===== File: envelope.cpp =====
Path: C:\Users\jindr\IthacaCore\sampler\envelopes\envelope.cpp

/*
 * envelope.cpp - ADSR envelope s fixnГғВӯmi parametry
 * REFAKTOROVГғВҒNO: OdstranГ„вҖәn per-MIDI kГғВіd, nahrazen fixnГғВӯmi ADSR parametry
 */

#include "envelope.h"
#include <algorithm>
#include <cstring>
#include <chrono>

/**
 * @brief PrГғВЎzdnГғВҪ konstruktor - vytvoГ…в„ўГғВӯ neinicializovanГғВҪ Envelope
 */
Envelope::Envelope() : attack_time_ms_(0.0f), decay_time_ms_(0.0f), 
                       sustain_level_(0.0f), release_time_ms_(0.0f),
                       sample_rate_index_(-1), bitrate_(0) {
    // Data se vygenerujГғВӯ aГ…Вҫ pГ…в„ўi volГғВЎnГғВӯ initialize()
}

/**
 * @brief Konstruktor s ADSR parametry
 */
Envelope::Envelope(float attack_ms, float decay_ms, float sustain_level, float release_ms)
    : attack_time_ms_(attack_ms), decay_time_ms_(decay_ms), 
      sustain_level_(sustain_level), release_time_ms_(release_ms),
      sample_rate_index_(-1), bitrate_(0) {
    
    // Validace parametrГ…ВҜ
    attack_time_ms_ = std::max(1.0f, attack_time_ms_);     // Min 1ms
    decay_time_ms_ = std::max(1.0f, decay_time_ms_);       // Min 1ms
    sustain_level_ = std::max(0.0f, std::min(1.0f, sustain_level_)); // 0.0-1.0
    release_time_ms_ = std::max(1.0f, release_time_ms_);    // Min 1ms
    
    // Data se vygenerujГғВӯ aГ…Вҫ pГ…в„ўi volГғВЎnГғВӯ initialize() nebo setEnvelopeFrequency()
}

/**
 * @brief Inicializace envelope dat s ADSR parametry
 */
void Envelope::initialize(Logger& logger, float attack_ms, float decay_ms, 
                         float sustain_level, float release_ms) {
    auto start_time = std::chrono::high_resolution_clock::now();
    
    logger.log("Envelope/initialize", "info", 
              "Starting ADSR envelope initialization with fixed parameters...");
    
    // NastavenГғВӯ parametrГ…ВҜ s validacГғВӯ
    attack_time_ms_ = std::max(1.0f, attack_ms);
    decay_time_ms_ = std::max(1.0f, decay_ms);
    sustain_level_ = std::max(0.0f, std::min(1.0f, sustain_level));
    release_time_ms_ = std::max(1.0f, release_ms);
    
    logger.log("Envelope/initialize", "info", 
              "ADSR Parameters - Attack: " + std::to_string(attack_time_ms_) + "ms, " +
              "Decay: " + std::to_string(decay_time_ms_) + "ms, " +
              "Sustain: " + std::to_string(sustain_level_) + ", " +
              "Release: " + std::to_string(release_time_ms_) + "ms");
    
    // Generuj envelope data pro oba sample rates
    generateAttackEnvelope();
    generateReleaseEnvelope();
    
    auto end_time = std::chrono::high_resolution_clock::now();
    auto duration_ms = std::chrono::duration_cast<std::chrono::milliseconds>(end_time - start_time).count();
    
    logger.log("Envelope/initialize", "info", 
              "ADSR envelope initialization completed in " + std::to_string(duration_ms) + "ms");
}

/**
 * @brief NastavГғВӯ frekvenci vzorkovГғВЎnГғВӯ
 */
void Envelope::setEnvelopeFrequency(int freq, Logger& logger) {
    bitrate_ = freq;
    
    if (freq == 44100) {
        sample_rate_index_ = 0;
        logger.log("Envelope/setEnvelopeFrequency", "info", 
                   "Envelope frequency set to 44100 Hz (index=0)");
    } else if (freq == 48000) {
        sample_rate_index_ = 1;
        logger.log("Envelope/setEnvelopeFrequency", "info", 
                   "Envelope frequency set to 48000 Hz (index=1)");
    } else {
        logger.log("Envelope/setEnvelopeFrequency", "error", 
                   "Invalid frequency " + std::to_string(freq) + " Hz - only 44100/48000 supported. Terminating.");
        std::exit(1);
    }
}

/**
 * @brief ZГғВӯskГғВЎ attack envelope data od zadanГғВ© pozice
 */
bool Envelope::getAttackGains(float* gainBuffer, int numSamples, sf_count_t position) const noexcept {
    if (sample_rate_index_ == -1 || !gainBuffer || numSamples <= 0) {
        // Fallback: vyplГ…ЛҶ 0.0f
        std::fill(gainBuffer, gainBuffer + numSamples, 0.0f);
        return false;
    }
    
    fillBufferFromFixedData(attack_envelope_, gainBuffer, numSamples, position, true);
    
    // Zkontroluj, zda envelope pokraГ„ВҚuje
    sf_count_t envelopeLength = getAttackLength();
    return (position + numSamples) < envelopeLength;
}

/**
 * @brief ZГғВӯskГғВЎ release envelope data od zadanГғВ© pozice
 */
bool Envelope::getReleaseGains(float* gainBuffer, int numSamples, sf_count_t position) const noexcept {
    if (sample_rate_index_ == -1 || !gainBuffer || numSamples <= 0) {
        // Fallback: vyplГ…ЛҶ 0.0f
        std::fill(gainBuffer, gainBuffer + numSamples, 0.0f);
        return false;
    }
    
    fillBufferFromFixedData(release_envelope_, gainBuffer, numSamples, position, false);
    
    // Zkontroluj, zda envelope pokraГ„ВҚuje
    sf_count_t envelopeLength = getReleaseLength();
    return (position + numSamples) < envelopeLength;
}

/**
 * @brief Getter pro dГғВ©lku attack envelope
 */
sf_count_t Envelope::getAttackLength() const noexcept {
    if (sample_rate_index_ == 0) {
        return attack_envelope_.len_44100;
    } else if (sample_rate_index_ == 1) {
        return attack_envelope_.len_48000;
    }
    return 0;
}

/**
 * @brief Getter pro dГғВ©lku release envelope
 */
sf_count_t Envelope::getReleaseLength() const noexcept {
    if (sample_rate_index_ == 0) {
        return release_envelope_.len_44100;
    } else if (sample_rate_index_ == 1) {
        return release_envelope_.len_48000;
    }
    return 0;
}

/**
 * @brief Generuje attack envelope pro oba sample rates
 */
void Envelope::generateAttackEnvelope() {
    std::vector<float> temp_data;
    
    // Generuj pro 44100 Hz
    generateEnvelopeForSampleRate(44100, true, temp_data, attack_envelope_.len_44100);
    attack_envelope_.data_44100 = std::make_unique<float[]>(attack_envelope_.len_44100);
    std::copy(temp_data.begin(), temp_data.end(), attack_envelope_.data_44100.get());
    
    // Generuj pro 48000 Hz
    generateEnvelopeForSampleRate(48000, true, temp_data, attack_envelope_.len_48000);
    attack_envelope_.data_48000 = std::make_unique<float[]>(attack_envelope_.len_48000);
    std::copy(temp_data.begin(), temp_data.end(), attack_envelope_.data_48000.get());
}

/**
 * @brief Generuje release envelope pro oba sample rates
 */
void Envelope::generateReleaseEnvelope() {
    std::vector<float> temp_data;
    
    // Generuj pro 44100 Hz
    generateEnvelopeForSampleRate(44100, false, temp_data, release_envelope_.len_44100);
    release_envelope_.data_44100 = std::make_unique<float[]>(release_envelope_.len_44100);
    std::copy(temp_data.begin(), temp_data.end(), release_envelope_.data_44100.get());
    
    // Generuj pro 48000 Hz
    generateEnvelopeForSampleRate(48000, false, temp_data, release_envelope_.len_48000);
    release_envelope_.data_48000 = std::make_unique<float[]>(release_envelope_.len_48000);
    std::copy(temp_data.begin(), temp_data.end(), release_envelope_.data_48000.get());
}

/**
 * @brief Generuje envelope data pro danГғВҪ sample rate
 */
void Envelope::generateEnvelopeForSampleRate(int sampleRate, bool isAttack, 
                                           std::vector<float>& output, int& numSamples) const {
    float time_ms = isAttack ? attack_time_ms_ : release_time_ms_;
    float time_seconds = time_ms / 1000.0f;
    
    // PoГ„ВҚet samples pro danГғВҪ Г„ВҚas
    numSamples = static_cast<int>(sampleRate * time_seconds);
    numSamples = std::max(1, numSamples);  // Min 1 sample
    
    output.resize(numSamples);
    
    // ExponenciГғВЎlnГғВӯ kГ…в„ўivka s tau = time_seconds / 3 (cca 95% za danГғВҪ Г„ВҚas)
    float tau = time_seconds / 3.0f;
    
    for (int i = 0; i < numSamples; ++i) {
        float t = (static_cast<float>(i) / static_cast<float>(numSamples - 1)) * time_seconds;
        
        if (isAttack) {
            // Attack: 0 ГўвҖ вҖҷ 1 exponenciГғВЎlnГ„вҖә
            output[i] = 1.0f - std::exp(-t / tau);
        } else {
            // Release: 1 ГўвҖ вҖҷ 0 exponenciГғВЎlnГ„вҖә
            output[i] = std::exp(-t / tau);
        }
        
        // Clamp na [0, 1]
        output[i] = std::max(0.0f, std::min(1.0f, output[i]));
    }
    
    // Truncate na threshold
    int converge_idx = -1;
    for (int i = 0; i < numSamples; ++i) {
        if (isAttack) {
            if (output[i] >= (1.0f - THRESHOLD)) {  // >= 0.99
                converge_idx = i;
                break;
            }
        } else {
            if (output[i] <= THRESHOLD) {  // <= 0.01
                converge_idx = i;
                break;
            }
        }
    }
    
    if (converge_idx > 0) {
        numSamples = converge_idx + 1;
        output.resize(numSamples);
    }
}

/**
 * @brief Helper: VyplnГғВӯ buffer s envelope daty
 */
void Envelope::fillBufferFromFixedData(const FixedEnvelopeData& env, float* gainBuffer, 
                                      int numSamples, sf_count_t position, bool isAttack) const noexcept {
    // Vyber sprГғВЎvnГғВЎ data podle sample rate
    const float* src_data;
    int len;
    
    if (sample_rate_index_ == 0) {
        src_data = env.data_44100.get();
        len = env.len_44100;
    } else {
        src_data = env.data_48000.get();
        len = env.len_48000;
    }
    
    if (len <= 1) {
        // SpeciГғВЎlnГғВӯ pГ…в„ўГғВӯpad pro velmi krГғВЎtkГғВ© envelope
        float constant_value = isAttack ? 1.0f : 0.0f;
        std::fill(gainBuffer, gainBuffer + numSamples, constant_value);
        return;
    }
    
    // RT-safe vyplnГ„вҖәnГғВӯ s clampem
    for (int i = 0; i < numSamples; ++i) {
        sf_count_t idx = position + static_cast<sf_count_t>(i);
        
        // Clamp idx na [0, len-1]
        if (idx >= len) {
            // Po konci envelope: konstantnГғВӯ target hodnota
            gainBuffer[i] = isAttack ? 1.0f : 0.0f;
        } else {
            gainBuffer[i] = src_data[static_cast<int>(idx)];
        }
    }
}


===== File: envelope.h =====
Path: C:\Users\jindr\IthacaCore\sampler\envelopes\envelope.h
=====
/*
 * envelope.h - RT-safe ADSR envelope s fixnГғВӯmi parametry
 * REFAKTOROVГғВҒNO: MГғВӯsto per-MIDI kГ…в„ўivek pouГ…ВҫГғВӯvГғВЎ fixnГғВӯ ADSR parametry
 * JednoduchГғВЎ konfigurace: attack_ms, decay_ms, sustain_level, release_ms
 * Position tracking pГ…в„ўesunut do Voice tГ…в„ўГғВӯdy pro lepГ…ВЎГғВӯ kontrolu
 */

#ifndef ENVELOPE_H
#define ENVELOPE_H

#include <cstdint>  // Pro uint8_t
#include "core_logger.h"  // Pro Logger
#include <sndfile.h>      // Pro sf_count_t (absolutnГғВӯ samples)
#include <vector>
#include <memory>
#include <cmath>

// Konstanty pro ADSR envelope
static constexpr float DEFAULT_ATTACK_MS = 500.0f;     // Default 500ms attack
static constexpr float DEFAULT_DECAY_MS = 300.0f;      // Default 300ms decay  
static constexpr float DEFAULT_SUSTAIN_LEVEL = 0.7f;   // Default 70% sustain
static constexpr float DEFAULT_RELEASE_MS = 1000.0f;   // Default 1000ms release
static constexpr float THRESHOLD = 0.01f;              // 99% convergence

/**
 * @class Envelope
 * @brief ADSR envelope s fixnГғВӯmi parametry pro vГ…ВЎechny MIDI noty
 * 
 * NOVГғВқ DESIGN:
 * - FixnГғВӯ ADSR parametry v milisekundГғВЎch
 * - Generuje pouze 2 kГ…в„ўivky (attack + release) mГғВӯsto 256 (128ГғвҖ”2)
 * - Position tracking v Voice, ne v Envelope
 * - KonfigurovatelnГғВ© parametry pro rГ…ВҜznГғВ© zvuky
 * - RT-safe metody bez MIDI parametru
 */
class Envelope {
public:
    /**
     * @brief Konstruktor s fixnГғВӯmi ADSR parametry
     * @param attack_ms Attack time v milisekundГғВЎch
     * @param decay_ms Decay time v milisekundГғВЎch  
     * @param sustain_level Sustain level (0.0-1.0)
     * @param release_ms Release time v milisekundГғВЎch
     */
    Envelope(float attack_ms, float decay_ms, float sustain_level, float release_ms);
             
    /**
     * @brief PrГғВЎzdnГғВҪ konstruktor pro delayed initialization
     * Envelope se vytvoГ…в„ўГғВӯ v neinicializovanГғВ©m stavu, musГғВӯ se zavolat initialize()
     */
    Envelope();

    /**
     * @brief Inicializace envelope dat s ADSR parametry
     * @param logger Reference na Logger pro logovГғВЎnГғВӯ
     * @param attack_ms Attack time v milisekundГғВЎch (default 500ms)
     * @param decay_ms Decay time v milisekundГғВЎch (default 300ms)
     * @param sustain_level Sustain level 0.0-1.0 (default 0.7)
     * @param release_ms Release time v milisekundГғВЎch (default 1000ms)
     */
    void initialize(Logger& logger, float attack_ms = DEFAULT_ATTACK_MS, 
                   float decay_ms = DEFAULT_DECAY_MS, float sustain_level = DEFAULT_SUSTAIN_LEVEL, 
                   float release_ms = DEFAULT_RELEASE_MS);

    /**
     * @brief NastavГғВӯ frekvenci vzorkovГғВЎnГғВӯ (44100 nebo 48000 Hz)
     * @param freq Frekvence v Hz
     * @param logger Reference na Logger
     */
    void setEnvelopeFrequency(int freq, Logger& logger);

    /**
     * @brief ZГғВӯskГғВЎ attack envelope data od zadanГғВ© pozice
     * @param gainBuffer Buffer pro vГғВҪstup
     * @param numSamples PoГ„ВҚet samples
     * @param position Pozice v envelope (spravuje Voice)
     * @return true pokud envelope pokraГ„ВҚuje
     */
    bool getAttackGains(float* gainBuffer, int numSamples, sf_count_t position) const noexcept;

    /**
     * @brief ZГғВӯskГғВЎ release envelope data od zadanГғВ© pozice
     * @param gainBuffer Buffer pro vГғВҪstup
     * @param numSamples PoГ„ВҚet samples
     * @param position Pozice v envelope (spravuje Voice)
     * @return true pokud envelope pokraГ„ВҚuje
     */
    bool getReleaseGains(float* gainBuffer, int numSamples, sf_count_t position) const noexcept;

    /**
     * @brief Getter pro sustain level
     * @return Sustain level (0.0-1.0)
     */
    float getSustainLevel() const noexcept { return sustain_level_; }

    /**
     * @brief Gettery pro dГғВ©lky envelope v samples pГ…в„ўi aktuГғВЎlnГғВӯ frekvenci
     */
    sf_count_t getAttackLength() const noexcept;
    sf_count_t getReleaseLength() const noexcept;

private:
    // FixnГғВӯ ADSR parametry v milisekundГғВЎch
    float attack_time_ms_;
    float decay_time_ms_;
    float sustain_level_;      // 0.0-1.0
    float release_time_ms_;
    
    // Frekvence management
    int sample_rate_index_ = -1;        // 0=44100, 1=48000, -1=nevalidnГғВӯ
    int bitrate_ = 0;                   // AktuГғВЎlnГғВӯ bitrate (Hz)
    
    // Simplified envelope data struktura
    struct FixedEnvelopeData {
        std::unique_ptr<float[]> data_44100;
        std::unique_ptr<float[]> data_48000;
        int len_44100;
        int len_48000;
        
        FixedEnvelopeData() : len_44100(0), len_48000(0) {}
        
        // Move konstruktor a assignment pro std::unique_ptr
        FixedEnvelopeData(FixedEnvelopeData&& other) noexcept 
            : data_44100(std::move(other.data_44100))
            , data_48000(std::move(other.data_48000))
            , len_44100(other.len_44100)
            , len_48000(other.len_48000) {}
        
        FixedEnvelopeData& operator=(FixedEnvelopeData&& other) noexcept {
            if (this != &other) {
                data_44100 = std::move(other.data_44100);
                data_48000 = std::move(other.data_48000);
                len_44100 = other.len_44100;
                len_48000 = other.len_48000;
            }
            return *this;
        }
        
        // ZakГғВЎzГғВЎnГғВӯ copy konstruktoru/assignment
        FixedEnvelopeData(const FixedEnvelopeData&) = delete;
        FixedEnvelopeData& operator=(const FixedEnvelopeData&) = delete;
    };
    
    FixedEnvelopeData attack_envelope_;
    FixedEnvelopeData release_envelope_;
    
    // GenerovacГғВӯ metody
    void generateAttackEnvelope();
    void generateReleaseEnvelope();
    void generateEnvelopeForSampleRate(int sampleRate, bool isAttack, 
                                      std::vector<float>& output, int& numSamples) const;
    
    // Helper metoda pro vyplnГ„вҖәnГғВӯ bufferu
    void fillBufferFromFixedData(const FixedEnvelopeData& env, float* gainBuffer, 
                                int numSamples, sf_count_t position, bool isAttack) const noexcept;
};

#endif  // ENVELOPE_H


===== File: ENVELOPE.md =====
Path: C:\Users\jindr\IthacaCore\sampler\envelopes\ENVELOPE.md
=====
### README.md pro tГ…в„ўГғВӯdu Envelope

#### ГғЕЎvod
TГ…в„ўГғВӯda `Envelope` slouГ…ВҫГғВӯ k RT-safe (real-time safe) vyplnГ„вҖәnГғВӯ bufferu gainy pro ADSR obГғВЎlky (attack a release) v audio sampleru. Data jsou naГ„ВҚtena z pre-computed const arrays v `envelopes.h` (generovГғВЎno Pythonem). TГ…в„ўГғВӯda podporuje dynamickou zmГ„вҖәnu sample rate (44100/48000 Hz) a pГ…в„ўГғВӯmou absolutnГғВӯ indexaci do polГғВӯ pro rychlГғВҪ lookup. LogovГғВЎnГғВӯ probГғВӯhГғВЎ v konstruktoru a pГ…в„ўi zmГ„вҖәnГ„вҖә frekvence. RT-safe: Г…ВҪГғВЎdnГғВ© alokace nebo sloГ…ВҫitГғВ© vГғВҪpoГ„ВҚty v runtime metodГғВЎch.

TГ…в„ўГғВӯda se integruje do `VoiceManager` (instanciace) a `Voice` (volГғВЎnГғВӯ v `calculateBlockGains` pro nahrazenГғВӯ lineГғВЎrnГғВӯho release).

#### Tabulka metod tГ…в„ўГғВӯdy Envelope

| Metoda                          | Popis                                                                 | Parametry                                                                 | NГғВЎvratovГғВҪ typ |
|---------------------------------|-----------------------------------------------------------------------|---------------------------------------------------------------------------|---------------|
| `Envelope(Logger& logger)`      | Konstruktor: NaГ„ВҚte data pro attack/release z envelopes.h, loguje informace o naГ„ВҚtenГғВҪch datech (128 MIDI, max len pro rates), validuje dГғВ©lku pro MIDI 127. Nenastavuje frekvenci. | `logger`: Reference na Logger pro logovГғВЎnГғВӯ.                               | `void` (konstruktor) |
| `void setEnvelopeFrequency(int freq, Logger& logger)` | NastavГғВӯ frekvenci (bitrate) a odpovГғВӯdajГғВӯcГғВӯ index (0/1), loguje zmГ„вҖәnu bitrate a index. Validuje jen 44100/48000 Hz, jinak error a exit(1). NastavГғВӯ private `bitrate_` a `sample_rate_index_`. | `freq`: Frekvence v Hz (44100 nebo 48000).<br>`logger`: Reference na Logger pro logovГғВЎnГғВӯ. | `void` |
| `void getGainBufferAttack(uint8_t midi, float* gainBuffer, int numSamples, sf_count_t start_elapsed) const noexcept` | VyplnГғВӯ `gainBuffer` gainy pro attack fГғВЎzi: PГ…в„ўГғВӯmГғВЎ indexace z attack_data_[midi], clamp na 0..len-1. Pro MIDI 0 (len=1): VyplnГғВӯ 1.0f. Fallback na 0.0f pГ…в„ўi chybГ„вҖә. | `midi`: MIDI hodnota (0-127).<br>`gainBuffer`: Buffer k vyplnГ„вҖәnГғВӯ.<br>`numSamples`: PoГ„ВҚet samples (napГ…в„ў. 512).<br>`start_elapsed`: Start samples od zaГ„ВҚГғВЎtku attack. | `void` |
| `void getGainBufferRelease(uint8_t midi, float* gainBuffer, int numSamples, sf_count_t start_elapsed) const noexcept` | VyplnГғВӯ `gainBuffer` gainy pro release fГғВЎzi: PГ…в„ўГғВӯmГғВЎ indexace z release_data_[midi], clamp na 0..len-1. Pro MIDI 0 (len=1): VyplnГғВӯ 0.0f. Fallback na 0.0f pГ…в„ўi chybГ„вҖә. | `midi`: MIDI hodnota (0-127).<br>`gainBuffer`: Buffer k vyplnГ„вҖәnГғВӯ.<br>`numSamples`: PoГ„ВҚet samples (napГ…в„ў. 512).<br>`start_elapsed`: Start samples od zaГ„ВҚГғВЎtku release. | `void` |

#### PГ…в„ўГғВӯklady volГғВЎnГғВӯ

##### 1. Instanciace v VoiceManager (v konstruktoru nebo initializeAll)
```cpp
// V voice_manager.cpp, v konstruktoru VoiceManager
Envelope::Envelope(Logger& logger) : envelope_(logger) {  // envelope_ je Г„ВҚlen tГ…в„ўГғВӯdy VoiceManager
    // Log: "Loaded attack/release data: 128 MIDI layers, max len 576001 samples for 44100 Hz and 48000 Hz. Frequency not set (bitrate=0, index=-1)."
    // Log: "Data validation OK - ready for setEnvelopeFrequency"
}

// Pak nastav frekvenci
envelope_.setEnvelopeFrequency(sample_rate_, logger);  // NapГ…в„ў. sample_rate_ = 44100
// Log: "Bitrate changed to 44100 Hz (index=0)"
```

##### 2. VolГғВЎnГғВӯ v programu (v calculateBlockGains Voice tГ…в„ўГғВӯdy)
PГ…в„ўedpoklГғВЎdГғВЎme, Г…Вҫe `Envelope& envelope_` je pГ…в„ўedГғВЎn do Voice z VoiceManager (napГ…в„ў. v konstruktoru Voice: `Voice(..., Envelope& envelope) : envelope_(envelope) {}`).

```cpp
// UpravenГғВЎ metoda v voice.cpp (nahrazuje lineГғВЎrnГғВӯ release)
bool Voice::calculateBlockGains(float* gainBuffer, int numSamples) noexcept {
    if (state_ == VoiceState::Idle || !gainBuffer || numSamples <= 0) {
        return false;
    }
    
    switch (state_) {
        case VoiceState::Sustaining:
        case VoiceState::Attacking: {
            // Constant gain for sustain/attack (nebo uprav pro attack envelope)
            const float constantGain = envelope_gain_;
            for (int i = 0; i < numSamples; ++i) {
                gainBuffer[i] = constantGain;
            }
            return true;
        }
        
        case VoiceState::Releasing: {
            // NOVГғвҖ°: NaГ„ВҚti envelope gain buffer pro celГғВҪ blok (absolutnГғВӯ indexace, MIDI parametr)
            const sf_count_t releaseElapsed = position_ - releaseStartPosition_;
            envelope_.getGainBufferRelease(release_midi_, gainBuffer, numSamples, releaseElapsed);  // release_midi_ = napГ…в„ў. 64
            
            // Aplikovat targetGain min (0.001f) na konec, pokud potГ…в„ўeba
            constexpr float targetGain = 0.001f;
            for (int i = 0; i < numSamples; ++i) {
                gainBuffer[i] = std::max(gainBuffer[i], targetGain);
            }
            
            // Update envelope_gain_ to last calculated value for getter consistency
            envelope_gain_ = gainBuffer[numSamples - 1];
            
            // Check if release is complete
            return envelope_gain_ > targetGain * 1.1f;
        }
        
        default:
            return false;
    }
}
```

#### Postup zmГ„вҖәn ve stГғВЎvajГғВӯcГғВӯm kГғВіdu
1. **PГ…в„ўidГғВЎnГғВӯ souborГ…ВҜ**: ZkopГғВӯruj `envelope.h` a `envelope.cpp` do sloГ…Вҫky `sampler/`. PГ…в„ўidej do `CMakeLists.txt`: `sampler/envelope.cpp sampler/envelope.h`.
2. **GenerovГғВЎnГғВӯ envelopes.h**: SpusГ…ВҘ Python `generate_envelopes.py` pro vytvoГ…в„ўenГғВӯ `envelopes.h` (include do envelope.h).
3. **Integrace do VoiceManager**: V `voice_manager.h` pГ…в„ўidej Г„ВҚlen `Envelope envelope_;`. V konstruktoru: `envelope_(logger);`. V `initializeAll`: `envelope_.setEnvelopeFrequency(sample_rate_, logger);`.
4. **Integrace do Voice**: V `voice.h` pГ…в„ўidej `Envelope& envelope_;` (reference). V konstruktoru Voice: `Voice(..., Envelope& envelope) : envelope_(envelope) {}`. V `VoiceManager::setNoteState`: PГ…в„ўedej envelope do voice.
5. **ГғЕЎprava calculateBlockGains**: NahraГ„ВҸ lineГғВЎrnГғВӯ release volГғВЎnГғВӯm `getGainBufferRelease` (viz pГ…в„ўГғВӯklad vГғВҪГ…ВЎe). Pro attack: NahraГ„ВҸ constant volГғВЎnГғВӯm `getGainBufferAttack`, pokud chceГ…ВЎ exponenciГғВЎlnГғВӯ nГғВЎrГ…ВҜst.
6. **Build a test**: Sestav projekt (`cmake --build build`), spusГ…ВҘ a sleduj logy v `core_logger/core_logger.log` (napГ…в„ў. "Loaded attack/release data...").

Toto umoГ…ВҫnГғВӯ snadnou integraci bez velkГғВҪch zmГ„вҖәn. Pokud potГ…в„ўebujeГ…ВЎ upravit pro decay/sustain, navrhni.

/*
THIS FILE IS LOCKED, IT IS FUNCTIONAL AND WILL NOT BE CHANGED

#include "core_logger.h"
#include <fstream>      // Pro std::ofstream a zГғВЎpis do souboru
#include <filesystem>   // Pro kontrolu adresГғВЎГ…в„ўe, vytvoГ…в„ўenГғВӯ sloГ…Вҫky a smazГғВЎnГғВӯ souboru (C++17)
#include <chrono>       // Pro zГғВӯskГғВЎnГғВӯ aktuГғВЎlnГғВӯho Г„ВҚasu
#include <iomanip>      // Pro formГғВЎtovГғВЎnГғВӯ Г„ВҚasu
#include <sstream>      // Pro sestavenГғВӯ stringu
#include <iostream>     // Pro std::cerr pГ…в„ўi chybГ„вҖә inicializace
#include <cstdlib>      // Pro std::exit
#include <string>       // Pro std::string
#include <cstdio>       // Pro printf

/**
 * @brief Konstruktor loggeru.
 * Kontroluje existenci a pГ…в„ўГғВӯstup k adresГғВЎГ…в„ўi, vytvГғВЎГ…в„ўГғВӯ sloГ…Вҫku core_logger,
 * smaГ…Вҫe existujГғВӯcГғВӯ log soubor a otevГ…в„ўe novГғВҪ v append mГғВіdu.
 * VГғВқSTUP: Vypisuje inicializaГ„ВҚnГғВӯ zprГғВЎvy na konzoli pomocГғВӯ printf.
 * @param path Cesta k adresГғВЎГ…в„ўi.
 * PГ…в„ўi selhГғВЎnГғВӯ: Tiskne chybu do std::cerr a volГғВЎ std::exit(1).
 */
Logger::Logger(const std::string& path) {
    printf("[Logger] Initializing logger subsystem...\n");
    printf("[Logger] Target directory: %s\n", path.c_str());
    
    std::filesystem::path dirPath(path);
    if (!std::filesystem::exists(dirPath)) {
        printf("[Logger] ERROR: Directory '%s' does not exist.\n", path.c_str());
        std::cerr << "Logger error: Directory '" << path << "' does not exist." << std::endl;
        std::exit(1);
    }
    if (!std::filesystem::is_directory(dirPath)) {
        printf("[Logger] ERROR: '%s' is not a valid directory.\n", path.c_str());
        std::cerr << "Logger error: '" << path << "' is not a valid directory." << std::endl;
        std::exit(1);
    }

    printf("[Logger] Directory validation: OK\n");

    // Kontrola pГ…в„ўГғВӯstupu k zГғВЎpisu (pokus o vytvoГ…в„ўenГғВӯ test souboru)
    printf("[Logger] Testing write access...\n");
    std::filesystem::path testFile = dirPath / "test_write.tmp";
    std::ofstream testStream(testFile);
    if (!testStream.is_open()) {
        printf("[Logger] ERROR: No write access to directory '%s'.\n", path.c_str());
        std::cerr << "Logger error: No write access to directory '" << path << "'." << std::endl;
        std::exit(1);
    }
    testStream.close();
    std::filesystem::remove(testFile);  // VyГ„ВҚiГ…ВЎtГ„вҖәnГғВӯ test souboru
    printf("[Logger] Write access: OK\n");

    // VytvoГ…в„ўenГғВӯ sloГ…Вҫky core_logger
    std::filesystem::path loggerDir = dirPath / "core_logger";
    printf("[Logger] Creating/verifying core_logger directory...\n");
    try {
        bool created = std::filesystem::create_directory(loggerDir);
        if (created) {
            printf("[Logger] Created new directory: %s\n", loggerDir.string().c_str());
        } else {
            printf("[Logger] Using existing directory: %s\n", loggerDir.string().c_str());
        }
    } catch (const std::filesystem::filesystem_error& e) {
        printf("[Logger] ERROR: Failed to create core_logger directory.\n");
        std::cerr << "Logger error creating core_logger directory: " << e.what() << std::endl;
        std::exit(1);
    }

    // Cesta k log souboru
    logFilePath_ = (loggerDir / "core_logger.log").string();
    printf("[Logger] Log file path: %s\n", logFilePath_.c_str());

    // SmazГғВЎnГғВӯ existujГғВӯcГғВӯho log souboru, pokud existuje
    if (std::filesystem::exists(logFilePath_)) {
        std::filesystem::remove(logFilePath_);
        printf("[Logger] Removed existing log file for clean start\n");
    }

    // OtevГ…в„ўenГғВӯ novГғВ©ho souboru v append mГғВіdu
    printf("[Logger] Opening log file for writing...\n");
    logFile_.open(logFilePath_, std::ios::app);
    if (!logFile_.is_open()) {
        printf("[Logger] ERROR: Cannot open log file '%s'.\n", logFilePath_.c_str());
        std::cerr << "Logger error: Cannot open log file '" << logFilePath_ << "'." << std::endl;
        std::exit(1);
    }

    // PoГ„ВҚГғВЎteГ„ВҚnГғВӯ zГғВЎznam v angliГ„ВҚtinГ„вҖә
    std::string initialLog = getTimestamp() + " [Logger/constructor] [info]: Logger initialized successfully at " + logFilePath_;
    logFile_ << initialLog << std::endl;
    logFile_.flush();  // OkamГ…ВҫitГғВҪ zГғВЎpis

    printf("[Logger] SUCCESS: Logger fully operational\n");
    std::string absolutePath = std::filesystem::absolute(logFilePath_).string();
    printf("[Logger] Log file can be found at: %s\n", absolutePath.c_str());
    printf("[Logger] To monitor logs in real-time, use: Get-Content -Path \"%s\" -Tail 10 -Wait\n", absolutePath.c_str());
}

/**
 * @brief Loguje zprГғВЎvu do souboru s timestampem.
 * Thread-safe: PouГ…ВҫГғВӯvГғВЎ mutex pro zГғВЎpis.
 * @param component NГғВЎzev komponenty.
 * @param severity ZГғВЎvaГ…Вҫnost.
 * @param message ZprГғВЎva.
 */
void Logger::log(const std::string& component, const std::string& severity, const std::string& message) {
    std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(logMutex_);  // Thread-safety

    if (!logFile_.is_open()) {
        return;  // Ignorovat, pokud soubor nenГғВӯ otevГ…в„ўenГғВҪ
    }

    std::string logEntry = "[" + getTimestamp() + "] [" + component + "] [" + severity + "]: " + message + "\n";
    logFile_ << logEntry;
    logFile_.flush();  // OkamГ…ВҫitГғВҪ zГғВЎpis pro debugging
}

/**
 * @brief ZГғВӯskГғВЎvГғВЎ aktuГғВЎlnГғВӯ timestamp ve formГғВЎtu YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM:SS.
 * @return FormГғВЎtovanГғВҪ timestamp jako std::string.
 */
std::string Logger::getTimestamp() const {
    auto now = std::chrono::system_clock::now();
    auto time_t = std::chrono::system_clock::to_time_t(now);
    std::tm timeStruct;
    localtime_s(&timeStruct, &time_t);  // BezpeГ„ВҚnГғВ© pro MSVC
    std::stringstream ss;
    ss << std::put_time(&timeStruct, "%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S");
    return ss.str();
}

/**
 * @brief Destruktor: Zaloguje ukonГ„ВҚenГғВӯ a uzavГ…в„ўe souborovГғВҪ stream.
 */
Logger::~Logger() {
    if (logFile_.is_open()) {
        // FinГғВЎlnГғВӯ zГғВЎznam pГ…в„ўed uzavГ…в„ўenГғВӯm
        std::string finalLog = getTimestamp() + " [Logger/destructor] [info]: Logger shutting down, closing log file";
        logFile_ << finalLog << std::endl;
        logFile_.flush();
        
        logFile_.close();
        
        // KonzolovГғВЎ zprГғВЎva o ukonГ„ВҚenГғВӯ
        printf("[Logger] Logger destructor called - log file closed\n");
    }
}

/*
THIS FILE IS LOCKED, IT IS FUNCTIONAL AND WILL NOT BE CHANGED
*/

#ifndef CORE_LOGGER_H  // Include guard pro prevenci duplikГғВЎtnГғВӯho includu
#define CORE_LOGGER_H

#include <string>       // Pro std::string
#include <mutex>        // Pro thread-safety pГ…в„ўi zГғВЎpisu
#include <fstream>      // Pro std::ofstream (definice logFile_)
#include <stdexcept>    // Pro vГғВҪjimky pГ…в„ўi chybГғВЎch (pouze internГ„вҖә)

/**
 * @class Logger
 * @brief JednoduchГғВҪ souborovГғВҪ logger bez JUCE zГғВЎvislostГғВӯ.
 * 
 * Loguje zprГғВЎvy s timestampem, komponentou a zГғВЎvaГ…ВҫnostГғВӯ do souboru core_logger.log.
 * Konstruktor bere cestu k adresГғВЎГ…в„ўi, kde vytvoГ…в„ўГғВӯ sloГ…Вҫku core_logger a log soubor.
 * PГ…в„ўi startu smaГ…Вҫe existujГғВӯcГғВӯ core_logger.log pro Г„ВҚistГғВҪ restart.
 * Thread-safe dГғВӯky mutexu. SelhГғВЎnГғВӯ inicializace vede k tisku do std::cerr a ukonГ„ВҚenГғВӯ programu.
 * 
 * DГ…В®LEГ…ВҪITГғвҖ°: Logger vypisuje inicializaГ„ВҚnГғВӯ zprГғВЎvy na konzoli (printf).
 * Pokud inicializace selГ…Вҫe, program se ukonГ„ВҚГғВӯ s exit(1).
 */
class Logger {
public:
    /**
     * @brief Konstruktor loggeru.
     * @param path Cesta k adresГғВЎГ…в„ўГғВӯ (absolutnГғВӯ nebo relativnГғВӯ, napГ…в„ў. "./").
     * Kontroluje existenci adresГғВЎГ…в„ўe a pГ…в„ўГғВӯstup; vytvГғВЎГ…в„ўГғВӯ sloГ…Вҫku core_logger a log soubor.
     * SmaГ…Вҫe existujГғВӯcГғВӯ core_logger.log, pokud existuje.
     * VГғВқSTUP: Vypisuje inicializaГ„ВҚnГғВӯ zprГғВЎvy na konzoli pomocГғВӯ printf.
     * PГ…в„ўi selhГғВЎnГғВӯ: Tiskne chybu do std::cerr a volГғВЎ std::exit(1).
     */
    explicit Logger(const std::string& path);

    /**
     * @brief Loguje zprГғВЎvu do souboru.
     * FormГғВЎt: [YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM:SS] [component] [severity]: message
     * @param component NГғВЎzev tГ…в„ўГғВӯdy/metody (napГ…в„ў. "SamplerIO/loadSamples").
     * @param severity ZГғВЎvaГ…Вҫnost (napГ…в„ў. "info", "error", "warn").
     * @param message ZprГғВЎva k logovГғВЎnГғВӯ.
     */
    void log(const std::string& component, const std::string& severity, const std::string& message);

    /**
     * @brief Destruktor: UzavГ…в„ўe souborovГғВҪ stream.
     */
    ~Logger();

private:
    std::string logFilePath_;  // Cesta k log souboru
    std::ofstream logFile_;    // SouborovГғВҪ stream pro zГғВЎpis
    mutable std::mutex logMutex_;  // Mutex pro thread-safety

    // PomocnГғВЎ metoda pro zГғВӯskГғВЎnГғВӯ timestampu
    std::string getTimestamp() const;
};

#endif  // CORE_LOGGER_H

#include "instrument_loader.h"
#include <cstdlib>      // Pro malloc, free, std::exit
#include <cstring>      // Pro memcpy
#include <sndfile.h>    // Pro sf_open, sf_readf_float, sf_close

/**
 * @brief PrГғВЎzdnГғВҪ konstruktor InstrumentLoader
 * Inicializuje vГ…ВЎechny hodnoty na vГғВҪchozГғВӯ stav.
 */
InstrumentLoader::InstrumentLoader()
    : actual_samplerate_(0), sampler_(nullptr), logger_(nullptr),
      totalLoadedSamples_(0), monoSamplesCount_(0), stereoSamplesCount_(0) {
    
    // Inicializace pole instruments - konstruktory Instrument se zavolajГғВӯ automaticky
    // (vГ…ВЎechny pointery na nullptr, velocityExists na false)
}

/**
 * @brief Destruktor - uvolnГғВӯ vГ…ВЎechnu alokovanou pamГ„вҖәГ…ВҘ
 * ProchГғВЎzГғВӯ vГ…ВЎechny MIDI noty a velocity vrstvy a uvolГ…ЛҶuje float buffery.
 * SampleInfo pointery se neuvolГ…ЛҶujГғВӯ (patГ…в„ўГғВӯ SamplerIO).
 */
InstrumentLoader::~InstrumentLoader() {
    // Destruktor volГғВЎ clear bez loggingu, protoГ…Вҫe nemГғВЎme garantovanou dostupnost loggeru
    clearWithoutLogging();
}

/**
 * @brief HlavnГғВӯ metoda pro naГ„ВҚГғВӯtГғВЎnГғВӯ dat instrumentГ…ВҜ
 * @param sampler Reference na SamplerIO pro pГ…в„ўГғВӯstup k sample metadatГ…ВҜm
 * @param targetSampleRate PoГ…ВҫadovanГғВЎ frekvence vzorkovГғВЎnГғВӯ (44100 nebo 48000 Hz)
 * @param logger Reference na Logger pro zaznamenГғВЎvГғВЎnГғВӯ
 */
void InstrumentLoader::loadInstrumentData(SamplerIO& sampler, int targetSampleRate, Logger& logger) {
    // Validace parametrГ…ВҜ
    validateSamplerReference(sampler, logger);
    validateTargetSampleRate(targetSampleRate, logger);
    
    // UloГ…ВҫenГғВӯ referencГғВӯ pro pozdГ„вҖәjГ…ВЎГғВӯ pouГ…ВҫitГғВӯ
    sampler_ = &sampler;
    logger_ = &logger;
    
    logger.log("InstrumentLoader/loadInstrumentData", "info", 
              "Starting loadInstrumentData with targetSampleRate " + 
              std::to_string(targetSampleRate) + " Hz");
    
    // AutomatickГғВ© vyГ„ВҚiГ…ВЎtГ„вҖәnГғВӯ pГ…в„ўedchozГғВӯch dat (pokud existujГғВӯ)
    if (actual_samplerate_ != 0) {
        logger.log("InstrumentLoader/loadInstrumentData", "info", 
                  "Clearing previous data (previous sampleRate: " + 
                  std::to_string(actual_samplerate_) + " Hz)");
        clear(logger);
    }
    
    // NastavenГғВӯ novГғВ© target sample rate
    actual_samplerate_ = targetSampleRate;
    
    logger.log("InstrumentLoader/loadInstrumentData", "info", 
              "InstrumentLoader initialized with targetSampleRate " + 
              std::to_string(actual_samplerate_) + " Hz");
    
    logger.log("InstrumentLoader/loadInstrumentData", "info", 
              "Prepared array for " + std::to_string(MIDI_NOTE_MAX + 1) + 
              " MIDI notes with " + std::to_string(VELOCITY_LAYERS) + " velocity layers");
              
    logger.log("InstrumentLoader/loadInstrumentData", "info", 
              "All samples will be converted to stereo interleaved format [L,R,L,R...]");
    
    // HlavnГғВӯ loading loop - stejnГғВҪ algoritmus jako pГ…ВҜvodnГғВӯ loadInstrument()
    logger.log("InstrumentLoader/loadInstrumentData", "info", 
              "Starting loading of all instruments for targetSampleRate " + 
              std::to_string(actual_samplerate_) + " Hz");
    
    int foundSamples = 0;
    int missingSamples = 0;
    totalLoadedSamples_ = 0;
    monoSamplesCount_ = 0;
    stereoSamplesCount_ = 0;
    
    // Cyklus pro vГ…ВЎechny MIDI noty 0-127
    for (int midi = MIDI_NOTE_MIN; midi <= MIDI_NOTE_MAX; midi++) {
        // Cyklus pro vГ…ВЎechny velocity 0-7
        for (int vel = 0; vel < VELOCITY_LAYERS; vel++) {
            // VyhledГғВЎnГғВӯ indexu v SamplerIO
            int index = sampler.findSampleInSampleList(
                static_cast<uint8_t>(midi), 
                static_cast<uint8_t>(vel), 
                actual_samplerate_
            );
            
            if (index != -1) {
                // Sample nalezen - naГ„ВҚtenГғВӯ do bufferu
                logger.log("InstrumentLoader/loadInstrumentData", "info", 
                          "Sample found for MIDI " + std::to_string(midi) + 
                          " velocity " + std::to_string(vel) + " at index " + std::to_string(index));
                
                // NaГ„ВҚtenГғВӯ samplu do bufferu
                if (loadSampleToBuffer(index, static_cast<uint8_t>(vel), static_cast<uint8_t>(midi), logger)) {
                    foundSamples++;
                    totalLoadedSamples_++;
                }
                
            } else {
                // Sample nenalezen - nastavenГғВӯ null a warning log
                instruments_[midi].sample_ptr_sampleInfo[vel] = nullptr;
                instruments_[midi].sample_ptr_velocity[vel] = nullptr;
                instruments_[midi].velocityExists[vel] = false;
                instruments_[midi].frame_count_stereo[vel] = 0;
                instruments_[midi].total_samples_stereo[vel] = 0;
                instruments_[midi].was_originally_mono[vel] = false;
                
                logger.log("InstrumentLoader/loadInstrumentData", "warn", 
                          "Sample for MIDI " + std::to_string(midi) + 
                          " velocity " + std::to_string(vel) + 
                          " not found at frequency " + std::to_string(actual_samplerate_) + " Hz");
                
                missingSamples++;
            }
        }
    }
    
    // Summary log s mono/stereo statistikami
    int totalSlots = (MIDI_NOTE_MAX + 1) * VELOCITY_LAYERS;
    logger.log("InstrumentLoader/loadInstrumentData", "info", 
              "Loading completed. Found: " + std::to_string(foundSamples) + 
              ", Missing: " + std::to_string(missingSamples) + 
              ", Total slots: " + std::to_string(totalSlots));
    
    logger.log("InstrumentLoader/loadInstrumentData", "info", 
              "Successfully loaded " + std::to_string(totalLoadedSamples_) + 
              " samples into memory as 32-bit stereo float buffers");
              
    logger.log("InstrumentLoader/loadInstrumentData", "info", 
              "Channel distribution: " + std::to_string(monoSamplesCount_) + 
              " originally mono, " + std::to_string(stereoSamplesCount_) + " originally stereo/multi-channel");
    
    // Validace stereo konzistence po naГ„ВҚtenГғВӯ
    logger.log("InstrumentLoader/loadInstrumentData", "info", 
              "Starting stereo consistency validation...");
    validateStereoConsistency(logger);
    
    logger.log("InstrumentLoader/loadInstrumentData", "info", 
              "InstrumentLoader data loading completed successfully");
}

/**
 * @brief VyГ„ВҚistГғВӯ vГ…ВЎechna naГ„ВҚtenГғВЎ data
 * @param logger Reference na Logger pro zaznamenГғВЎvГғВЎnГғВӯ
 * UvolnГғВӯ vГ…ВЎechny alokovanГғВ© float buffery a resetuje stav objektu.
 */
void InstrumentLoader::clear(Logger& logger) {
    int freedCount = 0;
    
    // ProchГғВЎzГғВӯ vГ…ВЎechny MIDI noty 0-127
    for (int midi = MIDI_NOTE_MIN; midi <= MIDI_NOTE_MAX; midi++) {
        // ProchГғВЎzГғВӯ vГ…ВЎechny velocity 0-7
        for (int vel = 0; vel < VELOCITY_LAYERS; vel++) {
            if (instruments_[midi].velocityExists[vel] && 
                instruments_[midi].sample_ptr_velocity[vel] != nullptr) {
                
                // UvolnГ„вҖәnГғВӯ float bufferu
                free(instruments_[midi].sample_ptr_velocity[vel]);
                instruments_[midi].sample_ptr_velocity[vel] = nullptr;
                instruments_[midi].velocityExists[vel] = false;
                
                // SampleInfo pointery se NEUVOLГ…вҖЎUJГғВҚ - patГ…в„ўГғВӯ SamplerIO
                instruments_[midi].sample_ptr_sampleInfo[vel] = nullptr;
                
                // Reset metadat
                instruments_[midi].frame_count_stereo[vel] = 0;
                instruments_[midi].total_samples_stereo[vel] = 0;
                instruments_[midi].was_originally_mono[vel] = false;
                
                freedCount++;
            }
        }
    }
    
    // Reset poГ„ВҚГғВӯtadel a stavu
    totalLoadedSamples_ = 0;
    monoSamplesCount_ = 0;
    stereoSamplesCount_ = 0;
    actual_samplerate_ = 0;
    
    logger.log("InstrumentLoader/clear", "info", 
              "Memory freed for " + std::to_string(freedCount) + " stereo buffers");
    logger.log("InstrumentLoader/clear", "info", 
              "InstrumentLoader data cleared and reset to uninitialized state");
}

/**
 * @brief VyГ„ВҚistГғВӯ vГ…ВЎechna naГ„ВҚtenГғВЎ data bez loggingu
 * PouГ…ВҫГғВӯvГғВЎ se v destruktoru kde logger nemusГғВӯ bГғВҪt dostupnГғВҪ.
 */
void InstrumentLoader::clearWithoutLogging() {
    // ProchГғВЎzГғВӯ vГ…ВЎechny MIDI noty 0-127
    for (int midi = MIDI_NOTE_MIN; midi <= MIDI_NOTE_MAX; midi++) {
        // ProchГғВЎzГғВӯ vГ…ВЎechny velocity 0-7
        for (int vel = 0; vel < VELOCITY_LAYERS; vel++) {
            if (instruments_[midi].velocityExists[vel] && 
                instruments_[midi].sample_ptr_velocity[vel] != nullptr) {
                
                // UvolnГ„вҖәnГғВӯ float bufferu
                free(instruments_[midi].sample_ptr_velocity[vel]);
                instruments_[midi].sample_ptr_velocity[vel] = nullptr;
                instruments_[midi].velocityExists[vel] = false;
                
                // SampleInfo pointery se NEUVOLГ…вҖЎUJГғВҚ - patГ…в„ўГғВӯ SamplerIO
                instruments_[midi].sample_ptr_sampleInfo[vel] = nullptr;
                
                // Reset metadat
                instruments_[midi].frame_count_stereo[vel] = 0;
                instruments_[midi].total_samples_stereo[vel] = 0;
                instruments_[midi].was_originally_mono[vel] = false;
            }
        }
    }
    
    // Reset poГ„ВҚГғВӯtadel a stavu
    totalLoadedSamples_ = 0;
    monoSamplesCount_ = 0;
    stereoSamplesCount_ = 0;
    actual_samplerate_ = 0;
}

/**
 * @brief NaГ„ВҚte jeden sample do bufferu
 * KompletnГғВӯ pipeline: otevГ…в„ўenГғВӯ souboru, alokace, naГ„ВҚtenГғВӯ, konverze, pГ…в„ўiГ…в„ўazenГғВӯ.
 * @param sampleIndex Index samplu v SamplerIO
 * @param velocity Velocity vrstva (0-7)
 * @param midi_note MIDI nota (0-127)
 * @param logger Reference na Logger pro zaznamenГғВЎvГғВЎnГғВӯ
 * @return true pГ…в„ўi ГғВәspГ„вҖәchu, false pГ…в„ўi chybГ„вҖә (s error logem a exit)
 */
bool InstrumentLoader::loadSampleToBuffer(int sampleIndex, uint8_t velocity, uint8_t midi_note, Logger& logger) {
    // Validace parametrГ…ВҜ
    validateVelocity(velocity, "loadSampleToBuffer", logger);
    validateMidiNote(midi_note, "loadSampleToBuffer", logger);
    
    // Krok 1: OtevГ…в„ўenГғВӯ souboru
    SNDFILE* sndfile = nullptr;
    SF_INFO sfinfo;
    
    if (!openSampleFile(sampleIndex, sndfile, sfinfo, logger)) {
        return false; // Chyba uГ…Вҫ je zalogovГғВЎna v openSampleFile
    }
    
    // ZГғВӯskГғВЎnГғВӯ metadat pГ…в„ўes SamplerIO gettery
    sf_count_t frameCount = sampler_->getSampleCount(sampleIndex, logger);
    int channelCount = sampler_->getChannelCount(sampleIndex, logger);
    bool needsConversion = sampler_->getNeedsConversion(sampleIndex, logger);
    bool isInterleaved = sampler_->getIsInterleavedFormat(sampleIndex, logger);
    const char* filename = sampler_->getFilename(sampleIndex, logger);
    
    // Krok 2: Alokace temporary bufferu pro naГ„ВҚtenГғВӯ (pГ…ВҜvodnГғВӯ velikost)
    size_t tempBufferSize = frameCount * channelCount * sizeof(float);
    float* tempBuffer = static_cast<float*>(malloc(tempBufferSize));
    
    if (!tempBuffer) {
        logger.log("InstrumentLoader/loadSampleToBuffer", "error", 
                   "Memory allocation error for temporary buffer: " + 
                   std::to_string(tempBufferSize) + " bytes");
        sf_close(sndfile);
        std::exit(1);
    }
    
    // Krok 3: NaГ„ВҚtenГғВӯ dat pomocГғВӯ sf_readf_float (automatickГғВЎ PCM->float konverze)
    sf_count_t framesRead = sf_readf_float(sndfile, tempBuffer, frameCount);
    sf_close(sndfile);
    
    if (framesRead != frameCount) {
        logger.log("InstrumentLoader/loadSampleToBuffer", "error", 
                   "Data reading error from file " + std::string(filename) + 
                   ": expected " + std::to_string(frameCount) + 
                   " frames, read " + std::to_string(framesRead));
        free(tempBuffer);
        std::exit(1);
    }
    
    // LogovГғВЎnГғВӯ konverze (vГ…Вҫdy, i kdyГ…Вҫ neprobГ„вҖәhla)
    if (needsConversion) {
        logger.log("InstrumentLoader/loadSampleToBuffer", "info", 
                   "PCM to 32-bit float conversion performed for file: " + std::string(filename));
    } else {
        logger.log("InstrumentLoader/loadSampleToBuffer", "info", 
                   "File already in 32-bit float format, no conversion needed: " + std::string(filename));
    }
    
    // Krok 4: NOVГғвҖ° - Alokace permanent bufferu VГғВқDY pro stereo (frameCount * 2 * sizeof(float))
    size_t stereoBufferSize = frameCount * 2 * sizeof(float);
    float* permanentBuffer = static_cast<float*>(malloc(stereoBufferSize));
    
    if (!permanentBuffer) {
        logger.log("InstrumentLoader/loadSampleToBuffer", "error", 
                   "Memory allocation error for permanent stereo buffer: " + 
                   std::to_string(stereoBufferSize) + " bytes");
        free(tempBuffer);
        std::exit(1);
    }
    
    // Krok 5: NOVГғвҖ° - Konverze na stereo formГғВЎt (monoГўвҖ вҖҷstereo duplikace nebo stereo kopГғВӯrovГғВЎnГғВӯ)
    bool wasOriginallyMono = (channelCount == 1);
    
    if (channelCount == 1) {
        // MONO ГўвҖ вҖҷ STEREO konverze: duplikace mono dat do obou kanГғВЎlГ…ВҜ (L=R)
        for (sf_count_t frame = 0; frame < frameCount; frame++) {
            permanentBuffer[frame * 2] = tempBuffer[frame];     // L kanГғВЎl
            permanentBuffer[frame * 2 + 1] = tempBuffer[frame]; // R kanГғВЎl (duplikace)
        }
        logger.log("InstrumentLoader/loadSampleToBuffer", "info", 
                   "Mono to stereo conversion performed (L=R duplication): " + std::string(filename));
        
    } else if (channelCount == 2) {
        // STEREO ГўвҖ вҖҷ STEREO: pГ…в„ўГғВӯmГғВ© kopГғВӯrovГғВЎnГғВӯ (jiГ…Вҫ sprГғВЎvnГғВҪ formГғВЎt)
        if (isInterleaved) {
            memcpy(permanentBuffer, tempBuffer, tempBufferSize);
            logger.log("InstrumentLoader/loadSampleToBuffer", "info", 
                       "Stereo data already in interleaved format, direct copy: " + 
                       std::string(filename));
        } else {
            // Non-interleaved ГўвҖ вҖҷ interleaved konverze
            for (sf_count_t frame = 0; frame < frameCount; frame++) {
                permanentBuffer[frame * 2] = tempBuffer[frame];                    // L kanГғВЎl
                permanentBuffer[frame * 2 + 1] = tempBuffer[frameCount + frame];   // R kanГғВЎl
            }
            logger.log("InstrumentLoader/loadSampleToBuffer", "info", 
                       "Non-interleaved to interleaved stereo conversion performed: " + 
                       std::string(filename));
        }
        
    } else {
        // Multi-channel (>2) ГўвҖ вҖҷ STEREO: pouГ…Вҫijeme jen prvnГғВӯ 2 kanГғВЎly
        if (isInterleaved) {
            // Interleaved multi-channel: [L1,R1,C1,L2,R2,C2...] ГўвҖ вҖҷ [L1,R1,L2,R2...]
            for (sf_count_t frame = 0; frame < frameCount; frame++) {
                permanentBuffer[frame * 2] = tempBuffer[frame * channelCount];     // L
                permanentBuffer[frame * 2 + 1] = tempBuffer[frame * channelCount + 1]; // R
            }
        } else {
            // Non-interleaved multi-channel: [L...][R...][C...] ГўвҖ вҖҷ [L1,R1,L2,R2...]
            for (sf_count_t frame = 0; frame < frameCount; frame++) {
                permanentBuffer[frame * 2] = tempBuffer[frame];                    // L kanГғВЎl
                permanentBuffer[frame * 2 + 1] = tempBuffer[frameCount + frame];   // R kanГғВЎl
            }
        }
        logger.log("InstrumentLoader/loadSampleToBuffer", "info", 
                   "Multi-channel to stereo conversion performed (using L+R channels): " + 
                   std::string(filename) + " (" + std::to_string(channelCount) + " ГўвҖ вҖҷ 2 channels)");
    }
    
    // Krok 6: UvolnГ„вҖәnГғВӯ temporary bufferu
    free(tempBuffer);
    
    // Krok 7: AKTUALIZACE - PГ…в„ўiГ…в„ўazenГғВӯ permanent bufferu, SampleInfo pointeru a NOVГғВқCH stereo metadat
    instruments_[midi_note].sample_ptr_velocity[velocity] = permanentBuffer;
    instruments_[midi_note].velocityExists[velocity] = true;
    
    // NOVГғвҖ°: UloГ…ВҫenГғВӯ stereo metadat
    instruments_[midi_note].frame_count_stereo[velocity] = frameCount;              // poГ„ВҚet stereo frame pГғВЎrГ…ВҜ
    instruments_[midi_note].total_samples_stereo[velocity] = frameCount * 2;       // celkovГғВҪ poГ„ВҚet float hodnot
    instruments_[midi_note].was_originally_mono[velocity] = wasOriginallyMono;     // pГ…ВҜvodnГғВӯ formГғВЎt
    
    // PoГ„ВҚГғВӯtГғВЎnГғВӯ mono/stereo statistik (podle pГ…ВҜvodnГғВӯho formГғВЎtu)
    if (wasOriginallyMono) {
        monoSamplesCount_++;
    } else {
        stereoSamplesCount_++;
    }
    
    // ZГғВӯskГғВЎnГғВӯ a pГ…в„ўiГ…в„ўazenГғВӯ SampleInfo pointeru (pointer na data v SamplerIO)
    // Pozor: Toto je trochu hacknutГғВ©, ale v kontextu souГ„ВҚasnГғВ©ho API je to nejjednoduГ…ВЎГ…ВЎГғВӯ
    // V ideГғВЎlnГғВӯm pГ…в„ўГғВӯpadГ„вҖә by SamplerIO mГ„вҖәlo getter getSampleInfo(index)
    const std::vector<SampleInfo>& sampleList = sampler_->getLoadedSampleList();
    if (sampleIndex >= 0 && static_cast<size_t>(sampleIndex) < sampleList.size()) {
        // Const cast kvГ…ВҜli designu - pointer na data v SamplerIO
        instruments_[midi_note].sample_ptr_sampleInfo[velocity] = 
            const_cast<SampleInfo*>(&sampleList[sampleIndex]);
    } else {
        logger.log("InstrumentLoader/loadSampleToBuffer", "error", 
                   "Invalid sampleIndex " + std::to_string(sampleIndex) + 
                   " for SampleInfo pointer assignment");
        std::exit(1);
    }
    
    // ГғЕЎspГ„вҖәГ…ВЎnГғВ© pГ…в„ўiГ…в„ўazenГғВӯ - detailnГғВӯ log s novГғВҪmi stereo metadaty
    logger.log("InstrumentLoader/loadSampleToBuffer", "info", 
               "Stereo buffer assigned for MIDI " + std::to_string(midi_note) + 
               " velocity " + std::to_string(velocity) + ": " + 
               std::to_string(frameCount) + " frames, " +
               std::to_string(frameCount * 2) + " total samples, " +
               std::to_string(stereoBufferSize) + " bytes, format: stereo interleaved [L,R,L,R...]");
    
    std::string originalFormat = wasOriginallyMono ? "originally mono" : "originally stereo";
    logger.log("InstrumentLoader/loadSampleToBuffer", "info", 
               "Buffer for MIDI " + std::to_string(midi_note) + 
               "/velocity " + std::to_string(velocity) + 
               " allocated and loaded successfully (" + originalFormat + ")");
    
    return true;
}

/**
 * @brief OtevГ…в„ўe sample soubor pro Г„ВҚtenГғВӯ
 * @param sampleIndex Index samplu v SamplerIO
 * @param sndfile Reference na SNDFILE pointer (vГғВҪstup)
 * @param sfinfo Reference na SF_INFO strukturu (vГғВҪstup)
 * @param logger Reference na Logger pro zaznamenГғВЎvГғВЎnГғВӯ
 * @return true pГ…в„ўi ГғВәspГ„вҖәchu, false pГ…в„ўi chybГ„вҖә (s error logem a exit)
 */
bool InstrumentLoader::openSampleFile(int sampleIndex, SNDFILE*& sndfile, SF_INFO& sfinfo, Logger& logger) {
    // ZГғВӯskГғВЎnГғВӯ cesty k souboru pГ…в„ўes SamplerIO getter
    const char* filename = sampler_->getFilename(sampleIndex, logger);
    
    // Inicializace SF_INFO struktury
    memset(&sfinfo, 0, sizeof(sfinfo));
    
    // OtevГ…в„ўenГғВӯ souboru pro Г„ВҚtenГғВӯ
    sndfile = sf_open(filename, SFM_READ, &sfinfo);
    
    if (!sndfile) {
        logger.log("InstrumentLoader/openSampleFile", "error", 
                   "File opening error " + std::string(filename) + 
                   ": " + sf_strerror(nullptr));
        std::exit(1);
    }
    
    logger.log("InstrumentLoader/openSampleFile", "info", 
               "File " + std::string(filename) + " opened successfully");
    
    return true;
}

/**
 * @brief Getter pro pГ…в„ўГғВӯstup k Instrument struktuГ…в„ўe podle MIDI noty
 * @param midi_note MIDI nota (0-127)
 * @return Reference na Instrument strukturu
 */
Instrument& InstrumentLoader::getInstrumentNote(uint8_t midi_note) {
    checkInitialization("getInstrumentNote");
    validateMidiNote(midi_note, "getInstrumentNote", *logger_);
    return instruments_[midi_note];
}

/**
 * @brief Const getter pro read-only pГ…в„ўГғВӯstup k Instrument struktuГ…в„ўe
 * @param midi_note MIDI nota (0-127)
 * @return Const reference na Instrument strukturu
 */
const Instrument& InstrumentLoader::getInstrumentNote(uint8_t midi_note) const {
    checkInitialization("getInstrumentNote const");
    validateMidiNote(midi_note, "getInstrumentNote const", *logger_);
    return instruments_[midi_note];
}

/**
 * @brief Getter pro celkovГғВҪ poГ„ВҚet naГ„ВҚtenГғВҪch samplГ…ВҜ
 * @return PoГ„ВҚet ГғВәspГ„вҖәГ…ВЎnГ„вҖә naГ„ВҚtenГғВҪch samplГ…ВҜ
 */
int InstrumentLoader::getTotalLoadedSamples() const {
    checkInitialization("getTotalLoadedSamples");
    return totalLoadedSamples_;
}

/**
 * @brief Getter pro poГ„ВҚet mono samplГ…ВҜ
 * @return PoГ„ВҚet naГ„ВҚtenГғВҪch mono samplГ…ВҜ
 */
int InstrumentLoader::getMonoSamplesCount() const {
    checkInitialization("getMonoSamplesCount");
    return monoSamplesCount_;
}

/**
 * @brief Getter pro poГ„ВҚet stereo samplГ…ВҜ  
 * @return PoГ„ВҚet naГ„ВҚtenГғВҪch stereo samplГ…ВҜ
 */
int InstrumentLoader::getStereoSamplesCount() const {
    checkInitialization("getStereoSamplesCount");
    return stereoSamplesCount_;
}

/**
 * @brief Validace, Г…Вҫe vГ…ВЎechny naГ„ВҚtenГғВ© buffery jsou skuteГ„ВҚnГ„вҖә stereo
 * @param logger Reference na Logger pro zaznamenГғВЎvГғВЎnГғВӯ
 * Kontroluje konzistenci mezi metadaty a skuteГ„ВҚnГғВҪmi buffery.
 * PГ…в„ўi selhГғВЎnГғВӯ validace: zaloguje chyby a volГғВЎ std::exit(1).
 */
void InstrumentLoader::validateStereoConsistency(Logger& logger) {
    checkInitialization("validateStereoConsistency");
    
    int validatedSamples = 0;
    int validationErrors = 0;
    
    for (int midi = MIDI_NOTE_MIN; midi <= MIDI_NOTE_MAX; midi++) {
        const Instrument& inst = instruments_[midi];
        
        for (int vel = 0; vel < VELOCITY_LAYERS; vel++) {
            if (inst.velocityExists[vel]) {
                validatedSamples++;
                
                // Kontrola 1: Buffer pointer nesmГғВӯ bГғВҪt null
                if (inst.sample_ptr_velocity[vel] == nullptr) {
                    logger.log("InstrumentLoader/validateStereoConsistency", "error", 
                              "NULL audio buffer for MIDI " + std::to_string(midi) + 
                              " velocity " + std::to_string(vel) + 
                              " despite velocityExists=true");
                    validationErrors++;
                    continue;
                }
                
                // Kontrola 2: SampleInfo pointer nesmГғВӯ bГғВҪt null
                if (inst.sample_ptr_sampleInfo[vel] == nullptr) {
                    logger.log("InstrumentLoader/validateStereoConsistency", "error", 
                              "NULL sampleInfo for MIDI " + std::to_string(midi) + 
                              " velocity " + std::to_string(vel) + 
                              " despite velocityExists=true");
                    validationErrors++;
                    continue;
                }
                
                // Kontrola 3: Frame count musГғВӯ bГғВҪt > 0
                if (inst.frame_count_stereo[vel] <= 0) {
                    logger.log("InstrumentLoader/validateStereoConsistency", "error", 
                              "Invalid frame_count_stereo " + std::to_string(inst.frame_count_stereo[vel]) + 
                              " for MIDI " + std::to_string(midi) + " velocity " + std::to_string(vel));
                    validationErrors++;
                }
                
                // Kontrola 4: Total samples musГғВӯ bГғВҪt frame_count * 2
                sf_count_t expectedTotalSamples = inst.frame_count_stereo[vel] * 2;
                if (inst.total_samples_stereo[vel] != expectedTotalSamples) {
                    logger.log("InstrumentLoader/validateStereoConsistency", "error", 
                              "Inconsistent total_samples_stereo for MIDI " + std::to_string(midi) + 
                              " velocity " + std::to_string(vel) + 
                              ": expected " + std::to_string(expectedTotalSamples) + 
                              ", got " + std::to_string(inst.total_samples_stereo[vel]));
                    validationErrors++;
                }
                
                // Kontrola 5: Konzistence s pГ…ВҜvodnГғВӯmi metadata (SampleInfo.sample_count)
                SampleInfo* sampleInfo = inst.sample_ptr_sampleInfo[vel];
                if (inst.frame_count_stereo[vel] != sampleInfo->sample_count) {
                    logger.log("InstrumentLoader/validateStereoConsistency", "error", 
                              "Frame count mismatch for MIDI " + std::to_string(midi) + 
                              " velocity " + std::to_string(vel) + 
                              ": stereo_frame_count=" + std::to_string(inst.frame_count_stereo[vel]) + 
                              ", original_sample_count=" + std::to_string(sampleInfo->sample_count));
                    validationErrors++;
                }
                
                // Kontrola 6: LogickГғВЎ konzistence was_originally_mono vs pГ…ВҜvodnГғВӯ channels
                bool expectedMono = (sampleInfo->channels == 1);
                if (inst.was_originally_mono[vel] != expectedMono) {
                    logger.log("InstrumentLoader/validateStereoConsistency", "error", 
                              "Mono flag inconsistency for MIDI " + std::to_string(midi) + 
                              " velocity " + std::to_string(vel) + 
                              ": was_originally_mono=" + (inst.was_originally_mono[vel] ? "true" : "false") + 
                              ", original_channels=" + std::to_string(sampleInfo->channels));
                    validationErrors++;
                }
            }
        }
    }
    
    // Summary validace
    logger.log("InstrumentLoader/validateStereoConsistency", "info", 
              "Stereo consistency validation completed. Validated " + std::to_string(validatedSamples) + 
              " samples, found " + std::to_string(validationErrors) + " errors");
    
    if (validationErrors == 0) {
        logger.log("InstrumentLoader/validateStereoConsistency", "info", 
                  "ГўЕ“вҖң All stereo buffers are consistent and valid");
    } else {
        logger.log("InstrumentLoader/validateStereoConsistency", "error", 
                  "ГўЕ“вҖ” Stereo consistency validation FAILED with " + 
                  std::to_string(validationErrors) + " errors - terminating");
        std::exit(1);
    }
}

/**
 * @brief Validuje velocity parametr
 * @param velocity Velocity hodnota k validaci
 * @param functionName NГғВЎzev funkce pro error log
 * @param logger Reference na Logger pro error log
 */
void InstrumentLoader::validateVelocity(uint8_t velocity, const char* functionName, Logger& logger) const {
    if (velocity >= VELOCITY_LAYERS) {
        logger.log("InstrumentLoader/" + std::string(functionName), "error", 
                   "Invalid velocity " + std::to_string(velocity) + 
                   " outside range 0-" + std::to_string(VELOCITY_LAYERS - 1));
        std::exit(1);
    }
}

/**
 * @brief Validuje MIDI note parametr
 * @param midi_note MIDI nota k validaci
 * @param functionName NГғВЎzev funkce pro error log
 * @param logger Reference na Logger pro error log
 */
void InstrumentLoader::validateMidiNote(uint8_t midi_note, const char* functionName, Logger& logger) const {
    if (midi_note < MIDI_NOTE_MIN || midi_note > MIDI_NOTE_MAX) {
        logger.log("InstrumentLoader/" + std::string(functionName), "error", 
                   "Invalid MIDI note " + std::to_string(midi_note) + 
                   " outside range " + std::to_string(MIDI_NOTE_MIN) + 
                   "-" + std::to_string(MIDI_NOTE_MAX));
        std::exit(1);
    }
}

/**
 * @brief Kontroluje inicializaci objektu
 * @param functionName NГғВЎzev funkce pro error log
 */
void InstrumentLoader::checkInitialization(const char* functionName) const {
    if (actual_samplerate_ == 0) {
        if (logger_) {
            logger_->log("InstrumentLoader/" + std::string(functionName), "error", 
                       "InstrumentLoader not initialized - call loadInstrumentData() first");
        }
        std::exit(1);
    }
}

/**
 * @brief Validuje referenci na SamplerIO
 * @param sampler Reference na SamplerIO k validaci
 * @param logger Reference na Logger pro error log
 */
void InstrumentLoader::validateSamplerReference(SamplerIO& sampler, Logger& logger) {
    // Pro C++ reference je teoreticky nemoГ…ВҫnГғВ©, aby byl nullptr,
    // ale pro jistotu mГ…ВҜГ…Вҫeme zkontrolovat adresu
    SamplerIO* samplerPtr = &sampler;
    if (samplerPtr == nullptr) {
        logger.log("InstrumentLoader/validateSamplerReference", "error", 
                  "SamplerIO reference is null - cannot proceed");
        std::exit(1);
    }
}

/**
 * @brief Validuje targetSampleRate
 * @param targetSampleRate Sample rate k validaci
 * @param logger Reference na Logger pro error log
 */
void InstrumentLoader::validateTargetSampleRate(int targetSampleRate, Logger& logger) {
    if (targetSampleRate != 44100 && targetSampleRate != 48000) {
        logger.log("InstrumentLoader/validateTargetSampleRate", "error", 
                  "Invalid targetSampleRate " + std::to_string(targetSampleRate) + 
                  " Hz - only 44100 Hz and 48000 Hz are supported");
        std::exit(1);
    }
}

Path: C:\Users\jindr\IthacaCore\sampler\instrument_loader.h

/*
THIS FILE IS LOCKED, IT IS FUNCTIONAL AND WILL NOT BE CHANGED
*/

#ifndef INSTRUMENT_LOADER_H  // Include guard pro prevenci duplikГғВЎtnГғВӯho includu
#define INSTRUMENT_LOADER_H

#include <cstdint>      // Pro uint8_t
#include <sndfile.h>    // Pro SNDFILE*, SF_INFO, sf_count_t
#include "sampler.h"    // Pro SamplerIO, SampleInfo, Logger
#include "core_logger.h" // Pro Logger (explicitnГғВӯ include pro jasnost)

// GlobГғВЎlnГғВӯ konstanty pro MIDI rozsah
#define MIDI_NOTE_MIN 0
#define MIDI_NOTE_MAX 127
#define VELOCITY_LAYERS 8  // Velocity 0-7

/**
 * @struct Instrument
 * @brief Reprezentuje jeden MIDI note (index 0-127) s vrstvami pro velocity 0-7.
 * 
 * Struktura uchovГғВЎvГғВЎ pointery na metadata (SampleInfo) a naГ„ВҚtenГғВЎ float data (RAM buffery)
 * pro vГ…ВЎechny velocity vrstvy jednГғВ© MIDI noty. Index v poli instruments[] odpovГғВӯdГғВЎ MIDI notГ„вҖә,
 * takГ…Вҫe nenГғВӯ potГ…в„ўeba uklГғВЎdat midi_note hodnotu v struktuГ…в„ўe.
 * 
 * DГ…В®LEГ…ВҪITГғвҖ°: VГ…ВЎechny buffery jsou VГғВқDY uloГ…Вҫeny jako stereo interleaved 32-bit float formГғВЎt!
 * I pГ…ВҜvodnГ„вҖә mono samples jsou konvertovГғВЎny na stereo (L=R duplikace).
 * Buffer formГғВЎt: [L1,R1,L2,R2,L3,R3,...] pro pГ…в„ўГғВӯmou JUCE kompatibilitu.
 */
struct Instrument {
    // Pointery na SampleInfo struktury z SamplerIO pro velocity 0-7
    // Tyto pointery odkazujГғВӯ na data vlastnГ„вҖәnГғВЎ SamplerIO (nesmГғВӯ se uvolГ…ЛҶovat)
    // POZOR: SampleInfo.channels obsahuje PГ…В®VODNГғВҚ poГ„ВҚet kanГғВЎlГ…ВҜ (1=mono, 2=stereo)
    SampleInfo* sample_ptr_sampleInfo[VELOCITY_LAYERS];
    
    // Pointery na naГ„ВҚtenГғВЎ float data v RAM pro velocity 0-7
    // Buffery jsou alokovanГғВ© pomocГғВӯ malloc a obsahujГғВӯ VГғВқDY stereo interleaved 32-bit float
    // Velikost: frame_count_stereo * 2 * sizeof(float) (vГ…Вҫdy stereo)
    // FormГғВЎt: [L1,R1,L2,R2,...] i pro pГ…ВҜvodnГ„вҖә mono samples (L=R)
    float* sample_ptr_velocity[VELOCITY_LAYERS];
    
    // IndikГғВЎtory existence samplu pro velocity 0-7
    // true = sample byl nalezen a naГ„ВҚten jako stereo, false = sample neexistuje
    bool velocityExists[VELOCITY_LAYERS];
    
    // NOVГғвҖ° METADATA - stereo informace (nezГғВЎvislГғВ© na SampleInfo)
    // PoГ„ВҚet stereo frame pГғВЎrГ…ВҜ (kaГ…ВҫdГғВҪ frame = L+R sample)
    sf_count_t frame_count_stereo[VELOCITY_LAYERS];
    
    // CelkovГғВҪ poГ„ВҚet float hodnot v bufferu (frame_count_stereo * 2)
    sf_count_t total_samples_stereo[VELOCITY_LAYERS];
    
    // IndikГғВЎtor pГ…ВҜvodnГғВӯho formГғВЎtu pГ…в„ўed konverzГғВӯ (true = byl mono, false = byl stereo)
    bool was_originally_mono[VELOCITY_LAYERS];
    
    /**
     * @brief Konstruktor - inicializuje vГ…ВЎechny pointery na nullptr a flags na false
     */
    Instrument() {
        for (int i = 0; i < VELOCITY_LAYERS; i++) {
            sample_ptr_sampleInfo[i] = nullptr;
            sample_ptr_velocity[i] = nullptr;
            velocityExists[i] = false;
            frame_count_stereo[i] = 0;
            total_samples_stereo[i] = 0;
            was_originally_mono[i] = false;
        }
    }
    
    /**
     * @brief Getter pro zaГ„ВҚГғВЎtek stereo bufferu
     * @param velocity Velocity vrstva (0-7)
     * @return Pointer na zaГ„ВҚГғВЎtek stereo float dat [L1,R1,L2,R2,...]
     * PГ…в„ўi neplatnГғВ©m velocity nebo neexistujГғВӯcГғВӯm samplu: nullptr
     */
    float* get_sample_begin_pointer(uint8_t velocity) const {
        if (velocity >= VELOCITY_LAYERS || !velocityExists[velocity]) {
            return nullptr;
        }
        return sample_ptr_velocity[velocity];
    }
    
    /**
     * @brief Getter pro poГ„ВҚet stereo frame pГғВЎrГ…ВҜ
     * @param velocity Velocity vrstva (0-7)
     * @return PoГ„ВҚet stereo frame pГғВЎrГ…ВҜ (kaГ…ВҫdГғВҪ frame = L+R sample)
     * PГ…в„ўi neplatnГғВ©m velocity nebo neexistujГғВӯcГғВӯm samplu: 0
     */
    sf_count_t get_frame_count(uint8_t velocity) const {
        if (velocity >= VELOCITY_LAYERS || !velocityExists[velocity]) {
            return 0;
        }
        return frame_count_stereo[velocity];
    }
    
    /**
     * @brief Getter pro celkovГғВҪ poГ„ВҚet float hodnot
     * @param velocity Velocity vrstva (0-7)
     * @return CelkovГғВҪ poГ„ВҚet float hodnot v bufferu (frame_count * 2)
     * PГ…в„ўi neplatnГғВ©m velocity nebo neexistujГғВӯcГғВӯm samplu: 0
     */
    sf_count_t get_total_sample_count(uint8_t velocity) const {
        if (velocity >= VELOCITY_LAYERS || !velocityExists[velocity]) {
            return 0;
        }
        return total_samples_stereo[velocity];
    }
    
    /**
     * @brief Getter pro informaci o pГ…ВҜvodnГғВӯm formГғВЎtu
     * @param velocity Velocity vrstva (0-7)
     * @return true pokud byl pГ…ВҜvodnГ„вҖә mono (pГ…в„ўed konverzГғВӯ), false pokud stereo
     * PГ…в„ўi neplatnГғВ©m velocity nebo neexistujГғВӯcГғВӯm samplu: false
     */
    bool get_was_originally_mono(uint8_t velocity) const {
        if (velocity >= VELOCITY_LAYERS || !velocityExists[velocity]) {
            return false;
        }
        return was_originally_mono[velocity];
    }
};

/**
 * @class InstrumentLoader
 * @brief Centralizuje naГ„ВҚГғВӯtГғВЎnГғВӯ WAV samplГ…ВҜ z SamplerIO do pamГ„вҖәti jako 32-bit float buffery.
 * 
 * TГ…в„ўГғВӯda automaticky konvertuje z PCM na float (podle getNeedsConversion) a na interleaved
 * formГғВЎt (podle getIsInterleavedFormat), s kompletnГғВӯm logovГғВЎnГғВӯm vГ…ВЎech konverzГғВӯ.
 * NaГ„ВҚГғВӯtГғВЎ pouze samples s poГ…Вҫadovanou frekvencГғВӯ vzorkovГғВЎnГғВӯ (targetSampleRate).
 * 
 * Inicializuje struktury pro vГ…ВЎechny MIDI noty (0-127) na zГғВЎkladГ„вҖә vГғВҪstupu scanSampleDirectory,
 * vГ„ВҚetnГ„вҖә not bez samplГ…ВҜ (null pointery + warning log).
 * 
 * PAMГ„ЕЎГ…ВӨOVГғВҒ SPRГғВҒVA:
 * - Alokuje buffery pomocГғВӯ malloc (C-style pro konzistenci)
 * - Automaticky uvolГ…ЛҶuje pГ…в„ўi novГғВ©m naГ„ВҚГғВӯtГғВЎnГғВӯ nebo v destruktoru
 * - SampleInfo pointery patГ…в„ўГғВӯ SamplerIO (neuvolГ…ЛҶujГғВӯ se)
 * 
 * BEZPEГ„Е’NOST:
 * - VГ…ВЎechny gettery kontrolujГғВӯ rozsah indexГ…ВҜ a inicializaci
 * - Chyby vedou k error logu a std::exit(1)
 * - Thread-safety nenГғВӯ implementovГғВЎna (single-threaded design)
 * 
 * NOVГғВқ DESIGN:
 * - PrГғВЎzdnГғВҪ konstruktor, data se naГ„ВҚГғВӯtajГғВӯ pomocГғВӯ loadInstrumentData()
 * - MoГ…Вҫnost opakovanГғВ©ho naГ„ВҚГғВӯtГғВЎnГғВӯ s rГ…ВҜznГғВҪmi targetSampleRate
 * - AutomatickГғВ© vyГ„ВҚiГ…ВЎtГ„вҖәnГғВӯ pГ…в„ўi novГғВ©m naГ„ВҚГғВӯtГғВЎnГғВӯ
 */
class InstrumentLoader {
public:
    /**
     * @brief PrГғВЎzdnГғВҪ konstruktor InstrumentLoader
     * 
     * Inicializuje pole instruments[128] na nullptr/false.
     * NastavГғВӯ actual_samplerate_ na 0 (indikuje neinicializovanГғВҪ stav).
     * Pro naГ„ВҚГғВӯtГғВЎnГғВӯ dat je tГ…в„ўeba zavolat loadInstrumentData().
     */
    InstrumentLoader();

    /**
     * @brief Destruktor - uvolnГғВӯ alokovanou pamГ„вҖәГ…ВҘ
     * 
     * ProchГғВЎzГғВӯ vГ…ВЎechny MIDI noty 0-127 a velocity 0-7:
     * - Pokud velocityExists[vel] == true, uvolnГғВӯ free(sample_ptr_velocity[vel])
     * - NEUVOLГ…вҖЎUJE SampleInfo pointery (patГ…в„ўГғВӯ SamplerIO)
     * - Zaloguje poГ„ВҚet uvolnГ„вҖәnГғВҪch samplГ…ВҜ (pokud je logger dostupnГғВҪ)
     */
    ~InstrumentLoader();

    /**
     * @brief HlavnГғВӯ metoda pro naГ„ВҚГғВӯtГғВЎnГғВӯ dat instrumentГ…ВҜ
     * @param sampler Reference na SamplerIO pro pГ…в„ўГғВӯstup k sample metadatГ…ВҜm
     * @param targetSampleRate PoГ…ВҫadovanГғВЎ frekvence vzorkovГғВЎnГғВӯ (44100 nebo 48000 Hz)
     * @param logger Reference na Logger pro zaznamenГғВЎvГғВЎnГғВӯ
     * 
     * Validuje parametry:
     * - Kontroluje platnost reference na sampler (nenГғВӯ nullptr)
     * - Kontroluje targetSampleRate (povoleno jen 44100 nebo 48000)
     * - PГ…в„ўi chybГ„вҖә loguje error a volГғВЎ std::exit(1)
     * 
     * Pokud uГ…Вҫ jsou data naГ„ВҚtenГғВЎ, automaticky je vyГ„ВҚistГғВӯ volГғВЎnГғВӯm clear().
     * PotГғВ© naГ„ВҚte vГ…ВЎechny MIDI noty 0-127 stejnГғВҪm algoritmem jako pГ…ВҜvodnГғВӯ loadInstrument().
     * 
     * Algoritmus:
     * 1. Validace parametrГ…ВҜ
     * 2. AutomatickГғВ© vyГ„ВҚiГ…ВЎtГ„вҖәnГғВӯ pГ…в„ўedchozГғВӯch dat (pokud existujГғВӯ)
     * 3. Pro kaГ…Вҫdou MIDI notu (MIDI_NOTE_MIN to MIDI_NOTE_MAX)
     * 4. Pro kaГ…Вҫdou velocity 0-7:
     *    a) VyhledГғВЎ index = sampler.findSampleInSampleList(midi, vel, targetSampleRate)
     *    b) Pokud index != -1:
     *       - ZavolГғВЎ loadSampleToBuffer(index, vel, midi) pro naГ„ВҚtenГғВӯ
     *       - NastavГғВӯ instruments[midi].velocityExists[vel] = true
     *    c) Pokud nenalezeno:
     *       - NastavГғВӯ null pointery, velocityExists[vel] = false
     *       - Warning log "Sample pro MIDI [midi] velocity [vel] nenalezen"
     * 
     * Loguje progress info a summary na konci.
     * UloГ…ВҫГғВӯ targetSampleRate do actual_samplerate_.
     */
    void loadInstrumentData(SamplerIO& sampler, int targetSampleRate, Logger& logger);

    /**
     * @brief Getter pro pГ…в„ўГғВӯstup k Instrument struktuГ…в„ўe podle MIDI noty
     * @param midi_note MIDI nota (0-127)
     * @return Reference na Instrument strukturu
     * 
     * Kontroluje inicializaci (actual_samplerate_ != 0).
     * Kontroluje platnost rozsahu MIDI noty.
     * PГ…в„ўi neinicializaci nebo neplatnГғВ©m rozsahu: log error a std::exit(1).
     */
    Instrument& getInstrumentNote(uint8_t midi_note);

    /**
     * @brief Const getter pro read-only pГ…в„ўГғВӯstup k Instrument struktuГ…в„ўe
     * @param midi_note MIDI nota (0-127)
     * @return Const reference na Instrument strukturu
     */
    const Instrument& getInstrumentNote(uint8_t midi_note) const;

    /**
     * @brief Getter pro zГғВӯskГғВЎnГғВӯ aktuГғВЎlnГғВӯ sample rate
     * @return Nastavenou actual sample rate v Hz (0 = neinicializovГғВЎno)
     */
    int getActualSampleRate() const { return actual_samplerate_; }

    /**
     * @brief Getter pro celkovГғВҪ poГ„ВҚet naГ„ВҚtenГғВҪch samplГ…ВҜ
     * @return PoГ„ВҚet ГғВәspГ„вҖәГ…ВЎnГ„вҖә naГ„ВҚtenГғВҪch samplГ…ВҜ
     * Kontroluje inicializaci - pГ…в„ўi neinicializaci loguje error a volГғВЎ std::exit(1).
     */
    int getTotalLoadedSamples() const;

    /**
     * @brief Getter pro poГ„ВҚet mono samplГ…ВҜ
     * @return PoГ„ВҚet naГ„ВҚtenГғВҪch mono samplГ…ВҜ
     * Kontroluje inicializaci - pГ…в„ўi neinicializaci loguje error a volГғВЎ std::exit(1).
     */
    int getMonoSamplesCount() const;

    /**
     * @brief Getter pro poГ„ВҚet stereo samplГ…ВҜ  
     * @return PoГ„ВҚet naГ„ВҚtenГғВҪch stereo samplГ…ВҜ
     * Kontroluje inicializaci - pГ…в„ўi neinicializaci loguje error a volГғВЎ std::exit(1).
     */
    int getStereoSamplesCount() const;

    /**
     * @brief Validace, Г…Вҫe vГ…ВЎechny naГ„ВҚtenГғВ© buffery jsou skuteГ„ВҚnГ„вҖә stereo
     * Kontroluje konzistenci mezi metadaty a skuteГ„ВҚnГғВҪmi buffery.
     * PГ…в„ўi selhГғВЎnГғВӯ validace: zaloguje chyby a volГғВЎ std::exit(1).
     * Kontroluje inicializaci - pГ…в„ўi neinicializaci loguje error a volГғВЎ std::exit(1).
     */
    void validateStereoConsistency(Logger& logger);

private:
    // AktuГғВЎlnГғВӯ frekvence vzorkovГғВЎnГғВӯ (0 = neinicializovГғВЎno)
    int actual_samplerate_;
    
    // Pointery na SamplerIO a Logger (uloГ…ВҫenГғВ© z poslednГғВӯho volГғВЎnГғВӯ loadInstrumentData)
    SamplerIO* sampler_;
    Logger* logger_;
    
    // Pole Instrument struktur pro MIDI noty 0-127
    // Index pole odpovГғВӯdГғВЎ MIDI notГ„вҖә
    Instrument instruments_[MIDI_NOTE_MAX + 1];
    
    // PoГ„ВҚГғВӯtadlo ГғВәspГ„вҖәГ…ВЎnГ„вҖә naГ„ВҚtenГғВҪch samplГ…ВҜ
    int totalLoadedSamples_;
    
    // PoГ„ВҚГғВӯtadla mono/stereo samplГ…ВҜ pro diagnostiku
    int monoSamplesCount_;
    int stereoSamplesCount_;

    /**
     * @brief VyГ„ВҚistГғВӯ vГ…ВЎechna naГ„ВҚtenГғВЎ data
     * @param logger Reference na Logger pro zaznamenГғВЎvГғВЎnГғВӯ
     * 
     * UvolnГғВӯ vГ…ВЎechny alokovanГғВ© float buffery pomocГғВӯ free().
     * Vynuluje vГ…ВЎechny pointery a poГ„ВҚГғВӯtadla.
     * Resetuje actual_samplerate_ na 0.
     * Loguje informace o uvolГ…ЛҶovГғВЎnГғВӯ.
     * 
     * VolГғВЎ se automaticky pГ…в„ўi novГғВ©m naГ„ВҚГғВӯtГғВЎnГғВӯ.
     */
    void clear(Logger& logger);

    /**
     * @brief VyГ„ВҚistГғВӯ vГ…ВЎechna naГ„ВҚtenГғВЎ data bez loggingu
     * 
     * StejnГғВЎ funkcionalita jako clear(), ale bez loggingu.
     * PouГ…ВҫГғВӯvГғВЎ se v destruktoru kde logger nemusГғВӯ bГғВҪt dostupnГғВҪ.
     */
    void clearWithoutLogging();

    /**
     * @brief NaГ„ВҚte jeden sample do bufferu
     * @param sampleIndex Index samplu v SamplerIO
     * @param velocity Velocity vrstva (0-7)
     * @param midi_note MIDI nota (0-127)
     * @param logger Reference na Logger pro zaznamenГғВЎvГғВЎnГғВӯ
     * @return true pГ…в„ўi ГғВәspГ„вҖәchu, false pГ…в„ўi chybГ„вҖә (s error logem a exit)
     * 
     * Algoritmus stejnГғВҪ jako v pГ…ВҜvodnГғВӯ verzi:
     * 1. OtevГ…в„ўe soubor pomocГғВӯ openSampleFile()
     * 2. Alokuje temporary buffer pro naГ„ВҚtenГғВӯ
     * 3. NaГ„ВҚte data pomocГғВӯ sf_readf_float (automatickГғВЎ PCM->float konverze)
     * 4. Alokuje permanent buffer pro interleaved data
     * 5. ZkopГғВӯruje/konvertuje na interleaved formГғВЎt (pokud potГ…в„ўeba)
     * 6. UvolnГғВӯ temporary buffer
     * 7. PГ…в„ўiГ…в„ўadГғВӯ permanent buffer a SampleInfo pointer do instruments_
     * 
     * Loguje vГ…ВЎechny konverze (i kdyГ…Вҫ neprobГ„вҖәhly) a ГғВәspГ„вҖәГ…ВЎnГғВ© pГ…в„ўiГ…в„ўazenГғВӯ.
     * PГ…в„ўi chybГ„вҖә alokace/naГ„ВҚtenГғВӯ: log error a std::exit(1).
     */
    bool loadSampleToBuffer(int sampleIndex, uint8_t velocity, uint8_t midi_note, Logger& logger);

    /**
     * @brief OtevГ…в„ўe sample soubor pro Г„ВҚtenГғВӯ
     * @param sampleIndex Index samplu v SamplerIO
     * @param sndfile Reference na SNDFILE pointer (vГғВҪstup)
     * @param sfinfo Reference na SF_INFO strukturu (vГғВҪstup)
     * @param logger Reference na Logger pro zaznamenГғВЎvГғВЎnГғВӯ
     * @return true pГ…в„ўi ГғВәspГ„вҖәchu, false pГ…в„ўi chybГ„вҖә (s error logem a exit)
     * 
     * PouГ…Вҫije getFilename(sampleIndex) pro zГғВӯskГғВЎnГғВӯ cesty.
     * OtevГ…в„ўe soubor pomocГғВӯ sf_open() v SFM_READ mГғВіdu.
     * PГ…в„ўi ГғВәspГ„вҖәchu: log info "Soubor [filename] otevГ…в„ўen ГғВәspГ„вҖәГ…ВЎnГ„вҖә"
     * PГ…в„ўi chybГ„вҖә: log error s sf_strerror() a std::exit(1)
     */
    bool openSampleFile(int sampleIndex, SNDFILE*& sndfile, SF_INFO& sfinfo, Logger& logger);

    /**
     * @brief Validuje velocity parametr
     * @param velocity Velocity hodnota k validaci
     * @param functionName NГғВЎzev funkce pro error log
     * @param logger Reference na Logger pro error log
     * 
     * Kontroluje rozsah 0-7. PГ…в„ўi neplatnГғВ© hodnotГ„вҖә: log error a std::exit(1).
     */
    void validateVelocity(uint8_t velocity, const char* functionName, Logger& logger) const;

    /**
     * @brief Validuje MIDI note parametr
     * @param midi_note MIDI nota k validaci
     * @param functionName NГғВЎzev funkce pro error log
     * @param logger Reference na Logger pro error log
     * 
     * Kontroluje rozsah MIDI_NOTE_MIN-MIDI_NOTE_MAX. PГ…в„ўi neplatnГғВ© hodnotГ„вҖә: log error a std::exit(1).
     */
    void validateMidiNote(uint8_t midi_note, const char* functionName, Logger& logger) const;

    /**
     * @brief Kontroluje inicializaci objektu
     * @param functionName NГғВЎzev funkce pro error log
     * 
     * Kontroluje actual_samplerate_ != 0. PГ…в„ўi neinicializaci: log error a std::exit(1).
     */
    void checkInitialization(const char* functionName) const;

    /**
     * @brief Validuje referenci na SamplerIO
     * @param sampler Reference na SamplerIO k validaci
     * @param logger Reference na Logger pro error log
     * 
     * Kontroluje, Г…Вҫe reference nenГғВӯ nullptr (teoreticky nemoГ…ВҫnГғВ© u referencГғВӯ,
     * ale pro jistotu). PГ…в„ўi chybГ„вҖә: log error a std::exit(1).
     */
    void validateSamplerReference(SamplerIO& sampler, Logger& logger);

    /**
     * @brief Validuje targetSampleRate
     * @param targetSampleRate Sample rate k validaci
     * @param logger Reference na Logger pro error log
     * 
     * Kontroluje, Г…Вҫe je 44100 nebo 48000. PГ…в„ўi chybГ„вҖә: log error a std::exit(1).
     */
    void validateTargetSampleRate(int targetSampleRate, Logger& logger);
};

#endif  // INSTRUMENT_LOADER_H

#include "sampler.h"
#include "voice_manager.h"  // Pro VoiceManager testing

// PodmГғВӯnГ„вҖәnГғВ© include pro testovacГғВӯ systГғВ©m
