# IthacaCore: C++ Sampler s Loggerem a InstrumentLoader

## Popis projektu
IthacaCore je profesionГғВЎlnГғВӯ audio sampler engine napsanГғВҪ v C++17. SystГғВ©m je modulГғВЎrnГғВӯ, s podporou logovГғВЎnГғВӯ (Logger), prohledГғВЎvГғВЎnГғВӯ WAV sample souborГ…ВҜ (SamplerIO), naГ„ВҚГғВӯtГғВЎnГғВӯ do pamГ„вҖәti jako stereo float buffery (InstrumentLoader) a koordinaci celГғВ©ho workflow (runSampler). **NOVГғвҖ°: PГ…в„ўidГғВЎna podpora pro voice management (Voice a VoiceManager) pro polyfonnГғВӯ pГ…в„ўehrГғВЎvГғВЎnГғВӯ s obГғВЎlkou a stavy (idle, attacking, sustaining, releasing).** NavrГ…Вҫen pro snadnou integraci do vГ„вҖәtГ…ВЎГғВӯch projektГ…ВҜ, jako je audio plugin nebo standalone aplikace. PouГ…ВҫГғВӯvГғВЎ libsndfile pro prГғВЎci s WAV soubory a podporuje parsovГғВЎnГғВӯ nГғВЎzvГ…ВҜ souborГ…ВҜ ve formГғВЎtu `mXXX-velY-fZZ.wav` (kde XXX je MIDI nota 0-127, Y je velocity 0-7, ZZ je zkrГғВЎcenГғВЎ frekvence s 'f' prefixem).

KlГғВӯГ„ВҚovГғВ© vlastnosti:
- Thread-safe logovГғВЎnГғВӯ do souboru
- ProhledГғВЎvГғВЎnГғВӯ metadat (frekvence, MIDI nota, velocity, dГғВ©lka, poГ„ВҚet kanГғВЎlГ…ВҜ) z WAV souborГ…ВҜ
- **NOVГғвҖ°: AutomatickГғВ© naГ„ВҚГғВӯtГғВЎnГғВӯ vГ…ВЎech samples do pamГ„вҖәti jako stereo interleaved float buffery**
- **NOVГғвҖ°: MonoГўвҖ вҖҷStereo konverze s duplikacГғВӯ dat (L=R) pro jednotnГғВҪ formГғВЎt**
- **NOVГғвҖ°: JUCE-ready buffer layout [L1,R1,L2,R2...] pro optimГғВЎlnГғВӯ audio processing**
- Detekce audio formГғВЎtu (interleaved/non-interleaved) a potГ…в„ўeby konverze do float
- AnalГғВҪza subformГғВЎtu (16-bit PCM, 24-bit PCM, 32-bit float, atd.)
- Validace konzistence frekvence mezi nГғВЎzvem souboru a obsahem
- VyhledГғВЎvГғВЎnГғВӯ sample podle MIDI noty a velocity
- PГ…в„ўГғВӯstup k metadatГ…ВҜm pГ…в„ўes bezpeГ„ВҚnГғВ© gettery (s kontrolou indexu)
- **NOVГғвҖ°: AutomatickГғВЎ validace stereo konzistence vГ…ВЎech naГ„ВҚtenГғВҪch bufferГ…ВҜ**
- **NOVГғвҖ°: Simulace JUCE AudioBuffer pro stereo vГғВҪstup bez zГғВЎvislosti na JUCE**
- Г…ВҪГғВЎdnГғВ© konzolovГғВ© vГғВҪstupy v modulech ГўвӮ¬вҖң vГ…ВЎe logovГғВЎno
- Detekce mono/stereo formГғВЎtu a dalГ…ВЎГғВӯ audio metadata
- **NOVГғвҖ°: PolyfonnГғВӯ voice management s obГғВЎlkou (attack/release) a stavy**

## PoГ…Вҫadavky
- Visual Studio Code
- Visual Studio 2022 Build Tools (s C++ komponentami) nebo Community Edition
- CMake (verze 3.10+, pГ…в„ўidejte do PATH)
- RozГ…ВЎГғВӯГ…в„ўenГғВӯ VS Code: CMake Tools a C/C++ od Microsoftu
- libsndfile (stГғВЎhne se automaticky pГ…в„ўes `add_subdirectory` v CMakeLists.txt)
- C++17 kompatibilnГғВӯ kompilГғВЎtor (MSVC/GCC/Clang)

## Postup nastavenГғВӯ
1. UloГ…Вҫte vГ…ВЎechny soubory do koГ…в„ўenovГғВ© sloГ…Вҫky projektu (napГ…в„ў. `IthacaCore`)
2. VytvoГ…в„ўte sloГ…Вҫku `.vscode` a uloГ…Вҫte do nГғВӯ `tasks.json`, `launch.json` a `settings.json`
3. VytvoГ…в„ўte sloГ…Вҫku `libsndfile` a stГғВЎhnГ„вҖәte do nГғВӯ zdrojovГғВҪ kГғВіd libsndfile (nebo pouГ…Вҫijte externГғВӯ build)
4. OtevГ…в„ўete projekt v VS Code (File ГўвҖ вҖҷ Open Folder)
5. SpusГ…ВҘte CMake: Configure (Ctrl+Shift+P ГўвҖ вҖҷ CMake: Configure). To vygeneruje build soubory v `build` sloГ…Вҫce

## SestavenГғВӯ a spuГ…ВЎtГ„вҖәnГғВӯ
- **SestavenГғВӯ**: SpusГ…ВҘte ГғВәlohu "build" (Ctrl+Shift+P ГўвҖ вҖҷ Tasks: Run Task ГўвҖ вҖҷ build). To nastavГғВӯ prostГ…в„ўedГғВӯ MSVC pГ…в„ўes `vcvars64.bat` a spustГғВӯ `cmake --build .`. VytvoГ…в„ўГғВӯ `Debug/IthacaCore.exe`
- **SpuГ…ВЎtГ„вҖәnГғВӯ**: KliknГ„вҖәte na tlaГ„ВҚГғВӯtko spustit (|> ) nebo stisknГ„вҖәte F5. Program se sestavГғВӯ a spustГғВӯ
- **VГғВҪstup**:
  - Na konzoli: ГғЕЎvodnГғВӯ zprГғВЎva "[i] Starting IthacaCore" a pГ…в„ўГғВӯpadnГ„вҖә parametry
  - V logu (`core_logger/core_logger.log`): ZГғВЎznamy o inicializaci loggeru, prohledГғВЎvГғВЎnГғВӯ sample, **NOVГғВқCH operacГғВӯch InstrumentLoader (naГ„ВҚГғВӯtГғВЎnГғВӯ do pamГ„вҖәti, monoГўвҖ вҖҷstereo konverze, validace)**, **NOVГғВқCH operacГғВӯch Voice/VoiceManager (inicializace voice, setNoteState, processBlock)**, vyhledГғВЎvГғВЎnГғВӯ (napГ…в„ў. "Loaded: m108-vel7-f44.wav (MIDI: 108, Vel: 7, Freq: 44100 Hz, Duration: 2.5s, Channels: 2 (stereo), Frames: 110250, Format: interleaved, needs float conversion)")
- **Г„Е’iГ…ВЎtГ„вҖәnГғВӯ**: SmaГ…Вҫte sloГ…Вҫku `build` a `core_logger` pro reset

**PoznГғВЎmka**: Cesta k `vcvars64.bat` v tasks.json je pro VS 2022 Build Tools. Pokud mГғВЎte Community, upravte na `C:\Program Files\Microsoft Visual Studio\2022\Community\VC\Auxiliary\Build\vcvars64.bat`. Pro PowerShell execution policy: `Set-ExecutionPolicy RemoteSigned -Scope CurrentUser`.

## PouГ…ВҫitГғВӯ v vlastnГғВӯm projektu
Pro integraci do vaГ…ВЎeho C++ projektu zahrГ…ЛҶte hlaviГ„ВҚky a linkujte libsndfile. PГ…в„ўГғВӯklad minimГғВЎlnГғВӯho pouГ…ВҫitГғВӯ (v main.cpp):
```cpp
#include "core_logger.h"
#include "sampler.h"
#include "instrument_loader.h"
#include "voice.h"           // NOVГғвҖ°: Pro Voice a VoiceManager
#include "voice_manager.h"   // NOVГғвҖ°: Pro polyfonnГғВӯ management
int main() {
    Logger logger("./"); // Cesta k logГ…ВҜm
    int result = runSampler(logger); // SpustГғВӯ celГғВҪ workflow vГ„ВҚetnГ„вҖә InstrumentLoader a VoiceManager
    return result;
}
```
Pro vlastnГғВӯ logiku pouГ…Вҫijte tГ…в„ўГғВӯdu `SamplerIO` (pro IO operace) a **NOVOU tГ…в„ўГғВӯdu `InstrumentLoader`** (pro naГ„ВҚГғВӯtГғВЎnГғВӯ do pamГ„вҖәti). **NOVГғвҖ°: Pro pГ…в„ўehrГғВЎvГғВЎnГғВӯ pouГ…Вҫijte `Voice` a `VoiceManager` pro polyfonii.** VГ…Вҫdy inicializujte `Logger` pro logovГғВЎnГғВӯ.

### PouГ…ВҫitГғВӯ tГ…в„ўГғВӯdy SamplerIO
`SamplerIO` pro Г„ВҚistГғВ© IO operace (prohledГғВЎvГғВЎnГғВӯ, vyhledГғВЎvГғВЎnГғВӯ, pГ…в„ўГғВӯstup k metadatГ…ВҜm). VytvoГ…в„ўte instanci a pГ…в„ўedejte logger.

| Metoda | Parametry | PГ…в„ўГғВӯklad | KomentГғВЎГ…в„ў | NГғВЎvratovГғВҪ typ | PГ…в„ўГғВӯklad nГғВЎvratu / Chyba |
|--------|-----------|---------|----------|---------------|-------------------------|
| `SamplerIO()` | - | `SamplerIO io;` | Konstruktor: Inicializuje prГғВЎzdnГғВҪ seznam `sampleList`. Г…ВҪГғВЎdnГғВ© logovГғВЎnГғВӯ v konstruktoru. | `void` (konstruktor) | - (Г…ВҫГғВЎdnГғВҪ nГғВЎvratovГғВҪ kГғВіd, ГғВәspГ„вҖәГ…ВЎnГғВЎ inicializace) |
| `~SamplerIO()` | - | AutomatickГғВҪ | Destruktor: Г…ВҪГғВЎdnГғВ© speciГғВЎlnГғВӯ akce (seznam se uvolnГғВӯ automaticky). | `void` (destruktor) | - (automatickГғВ© uvolnГ„вҖәnГғВӯ) |
| `scanSampleDirectory(const std::string& directoryPath, Logger& logger)` | `directoryPath` ГўвӮ¬вҖң cesta k adresГғВЎГ…в„ўi se WAV soubory (napГ…в„ў. `"./samples"`), `logger` ГўвӮ¬вҖң reference na Logger | `io.scanSampleDirectory(R"(c:\samples)", logger);` | ProhledГғВЎ adresГғВЎГ…в„ў. Deleguje parsovГғВЎnГғВӯ nГғВЎzvГ…ВҜ (regex), naГ„ВҚte metadata (libsndfile). Validuje konzistenci frekvence mezi nГғВЎzvem a souborem. Detekuje formГғВЎt (interleaved) a potГ…в„ўebu konverze (PCMГўвҖ вҖҷfloat). Loguje info/warn/error. Chyby (neexistujГғВӯcГғВӯ adresГғВЎГ…в„ў, nekonzistentnГғВӯ frekvence): zaloguje a `std::exit(1)`. | `void` | - (ГғВәspГ„вҖәch: naГ„ВҚte data; chyba: exit(1) po logu) |
| `findSampleInSampleList(uint8_t midi_note, uint8_t velocity, int sampleRate) const` | `midi_note` (0-127), `velocity` (0-7), `sampleRate` (frekvence v Hz) | `int idx = io.findSampleInSampleList(60, 5, 44100);` | VyhledГғВЎ index sample v internГғВӯm seznamu. VrГғВЎtГғВӯ -1, pokud nenalezeno. LineГғВЎrnГғВӯ prohledГғВЎvГғВЎnГғВӯ, Г…ВҫГғВЎdnГғВ© logovГғВЎnГғВӯ. | `int` | `0` (index prvnГғВӯ shody); `-1` (nenalezeno, nenГғВӯ chyba) |
| `getLoadedSampleList() const` | - | `const auto& list = io.getLoadedSampleList();` | VrГғВЎtГғВӯ konstantnГғВӯ referenci na vektor `SampleInfo` pro Г„ВҚtenГғВӯ metadat. Г…ВҪГғВЎdnГғВ© logovГғВЎnГғВӯ. | `const std::vector<SampleInfo>&` | Reference na vektor (prГғВЎzdnГғВҪ, pokud nenГғВӯ naГ„ВҚteno) |

### **NOVГғвҖ°: PouГ…ВҫitГғВӯ tГ…в„ўГғВӯdy InstrumentLoader**
`InstrumentLoader` pro naГ„ВҚГғВӯtГғВЎnГғВӯ WAV samples do pamГ„вҖәti jako 32-bit stereo float buffery optimalizovanГғВ© pro JUCE. **KlГғВӯГ„ВҚovГғВЎ novГғВЎ funkcionalita:**

#### **HlavnГғВӯ vlastnosti:**
- **PovinnГғВЎ stereo konverze**: VГ…ВЎechny samples (i pГ…ВҜvodnГ„вҖә mono) jsou uloГ…Вҫeny jako stereo `[L1,R1,L2,R2...]`
- **MonoГўвҖ вҖҷStereo duplikace**: Mono samples se automaticky duplikujГғВӯ do obou kanГғВЎlГ…ВҜ (L=R)
- **JUCE-ready formГғВЎt**: Buffer layout optimalizovanГғВҪ pro JUCE AudioBuffer de-interleaving
- **AutomatickГғВЎ validace**: Kontrola konzistence vГ…ВЎech naГ„ВҚtenГғВҪch bufferГ…ВҜ
- **FiltrovГғВЎnГғВӯ frekvence**: NaГ„ВҚГғВӯtГғВЎ pouze samples s poГ…Вҫadovanou frekvencГғВӯ vzorkovГғВЎnГғВӯ

| Metoda | Parametry | PГ…в„ўГғВӯklad | KomentГғВЎГ…в„ў | NГғВЎvratovГғВҪ typ |
|--------|-----------|---------|----------|---------------|
| `InstrumentLoader(SamplerIO& sampler, int targetSampleRate, Logger& logger)` | `sampler` ГўвӮ¬вҖң reference na SamplerIO, `targetSampleRate` ГўвӮ¬вҖң poГ…ВҫadovanГғВЎ frekvence (napГ…в„ў. 44100), `logger` ГўвӮ¬вҖң reference na Logger | `InstrumentLoader loader(sampler, 44100, logger);` | Konstruktor: Inicializuje pole pro vГ…ВЎechny MIDI noty 0-127. Loguje inicializaci s targetSampleRate. | `void` (konstruktor) |
| `loadInstrument()` | - | `loader.loadInstrument();` | **HLAVNГғВҚ METODA**: NaГ„ВҚte vГ…ВЎechny dostupnГғВ© samples do pamГ„вҖәti jako stereo float buffery. ProchГғВЎzГғВӯ vГ…ВЎechny MIDI noty 0-127 a velocity 0-7. ProvГғВЎdГғВӯ monoГўвҖ вҖҷstereo konverzi. Validuje konzistenci po naГ„ВҚtenГғВӯ. Loguje progress a statistiky. | `void` |
| `getInstrumentNote(uint8_t midi_note)` | `midi_note` (0-127) | `Instrument& inst = loader.getInstrumentNote(108);` | VrГғВЎtГғВӯ referenci na Instrument strukturu pro danou MIDI notu. Kontroluje platnost rozsahu. PГ…в„ўi chybГ„вҖә: log error a exit(1). | `Instrument&` |
| `getTotalLoadedSamples()` | - | `int total = loader.getTotalLoadedSamples();` | Getter pro celkovГғВҪ poГ„ВҚet ГғВәspГ„вҖәГ…ВЎnГ„вҖә naГ„ВҚtenГғВҪch samples. | `int` |
| `getMonoSamplesCount()` | - | `int mono = loader.getMonoSamplesCount();` | Getter pro poГ„ВҚet pГ…ВҜvodnГ„вҖә mono samples (pГ…в„ўed konverzГғВӯ na stereo). | `int` |
| `getStereoSamplesCount()` | - | `int stereo = loader.getStereoSamplesCount();` | Getter pro poГ„ВҚet pГ…ВҜvodnГ„вҖә stereo samples. | `int` |
| `getTargetSampleRate()` | - | `int rate = loader.getTargetSampleRate();` | Getter pro nastavenou target sample rate v Hz. | `int` |

#### **NOVГғВҒ struktura Instrument s API metodami:**
```cpp
struct Instrument {
    // ExistujГғВӯcГғВӯ pole
    SampleInfo* sample_ptr_sampleInfo[8];    // pointery na SampleInfo
    float* sample_ptr_velocity[8];           // pointery na stereo float buffery
    bool velocityExists[8];                  // indikГғВЎtory existence
    
    // NOVГғВҒ metadata
    sf_count_t frame_count_stereo[8];        // poГ„ВҚet stereo frame pГғВЎrГ…ВҜ
    sf_count_t total_samples_stereo[8];      // celkovГғВҪ poГ„ВҚet float hodnot (frame_count * 2)
    bool was_originally_mono[8];             // pГ…ВҜvodnГғВӯ formГғВЎt pГ…в„ўed konverzГғВӯ
    
    // NOVГғвҖ° API metody pro pГ…в„ўГғВӯstup k stereo datГ…ВҜm
    float* get_sample_begin_pointer(uint8_t velocity);    // pointer na stereo data [L,R,L,R...]
    sf_count_t get_frame_count(uint8_t velocity);         // poГ„ВҚet stereo frame pГғВЎrГ…ВҜ
    sf_count_t get_total_sample_count(uint8_t velocity);  // celkovГғВҪ poГ„ВҚet float hodnot
    bool get_was_originally_mono(uint8_t velocity);       // pГ…ВҜvodnГғВӯ formГғВЎt info
};
```

#### **PГ…в„ўГғВӯklad kompletnГғВӯho pouГ…ВҫitГғВӯ s InstrumentLoader:**
```cpp
Logger logger("./");
SamplerIO sampler;
std::string dir = R"(c:\Users\jindr\AppData\Roaming\IthacaPlayer\instrument)";

// 1. ProhledГғВЎnГғВӯ adresГғВЎГ…в„ўe
sampler.scanSampleDirectory(dir, logger);

// 2. NOVГғвҖ°: NaГ„ВҚtenГғВӯ vГ…ВЎech samples do pamГ„вҖәti jako stereo buffery
InstrumentLoader loader(sampler, 44100, logger);
loader.loadInstrument();  // AutomatickГғВЎ monoГўвҖ вҖҷstereo konverze a validace

// 3. NOVГғвҖ°: PГ…в„ўГғВӯstup k naГ„ВҚtenГғВҪm stereo datГ…ВҜm
Instrument& inst = loader.getInstrumentNote(108);
if (inst.velocityExists[7]) {
    // ZГғВӯskГғВЎnГғВӯ stereo dat ready pro JUCE
    float* stereoData = inst.get_sample_begin_pointer(7);      // [L1,R1,L2,R2...]
    sf_count_t frames = inst.get_frame_count(7);               // poГ„ВҚet stereo pГғВЎrГ…ВҜ
    sf_count_t totalSamples = inst.get_total_sample_count(7);  // celkovГғВҪ poГ„ВҚet float hodnot
    bool wasMono = inst.get_was_originally_mono(7);            // pГ…ВҜvodnГғВӯ formГғВЎt
    
    // Pro JUCE AudioBuffer de-interleaving:
    /*
    AudioBuffer<float> juceBuffer(2, frames); // 2 kanГғВЎly
    float* leftChannel = juceBuffer.getWritePointer(0);
    float* rightChannel = juceBuffer.getWritePointer(1);
    
    for (int frame = 0; frame < frames; frame++) {
        leftChannel[frame] = stereoData[frame * 2];     // L kanГғВЎl
        rightChannel[frame] = stereoData[frame * 2 + 1]; // R kanГғВЎl
    }
    */
}

// 4. NOVГғвҖ°: Statistiky naГ„ВҚГғВӯtГғВЎnГғВӯ
logger.log("demo", "info", "Total loaded: " + std::to_string(loader.getTotalLoadedSamples()));
logger.log("demo", "info", "Originally mono: " + std::to_string(loader.getMonoSamplesCount()));
logger.log("demo", "info", "Originally stereo: " + std::to_string(loader.getStereoSamplesCount()));
```

### **NOVГғвҖ°: PouГ…ВҫitГғВӯ tГ…в„ўГғВӯdy Voice a VoiceManager**
`Voice` reprezentuje jednu hlasovou jednotku pro pГ…в„ўehrГғВЎvГғВЎnГғВӯ sample s obГғВЎlkou (attack/release) a stavy (idle, attacking, sustaining, releasing). `VoiceManager` spravuje pool voice pro polyfonii (napГ…в„ў. 128 hlasГ…ВҜ). PouГ…ВҫГғВӯvГғВЎ simulaci `AudioBuffer` pro stereo vГғВҪstup bez zГғВЎvislosti na JUCE.

#### **HlavnГғВӯ vlastnosti:**
- **Polyfonie**: VoiceManager pГ…в„ўiГ…в„ўazuje MIDI noty k volnГғВҪm voices.
- **ObГғВЎlka**: JednoduchГғВЎ time-based gain (release 200 ms).
- **Stavy**: Enum `VoiceState` pro Г…в„ўГғВӯzenГғВӯ lifecycle (startNote/stopNote).
- **AudioBuffer**: Simulace JUCE bufferu pro vГғВҪstup [left, right].
- **AudioData**: Struktura pro jeden stereo sample.

#### **Tabulka metod Voice:**
| Metoda | Parametry | PГ…в„ўГғВӯklad | KomentГғВЎГ…в„ў | NГғВЎvratovГғВҪ typ |
|--------|-----------|---------|----------|---------------|
| `Voice()` | - | `Voice voice;` | Default konstruktor: Inicializuje idle stav (pro pool v VoiceManager). | `void` (konstruktor) |
| `Voice(uint8_t midiNote, Logger& logger)` | `midiNote` (0-127), `logger` | `Voice voice(60, logger);` | Konstruktor pro VoiceManager: NastavГғВӯ MIDI notu, instrument pozdГ„вҖәji pГ…в„ўes initialize. | `void` (konstruktor) |
| `Voice(uint8_t midiNote, const Instrument& instrument, Logger& logger)` | `midiNote`, `instrument`, `logger` | `Voice voice(60, inst, logger);` | PlnГғВҪ konstruktor: Inicializuje s instrumentem. | `void` (konstruktor) |
| `initialize(const Instrument& instrument)` | `instrument` | `voice.initialize(inst);` | Inicializuje s instrumentem (pro pool). | `void` |
| `cleanup()` | - | `voice.cleanup();` | Reset na idle stav. | `void` |
| `reinitialize(const Instrument& instrument)` | `instrument` | `voice.reinitialize(inst);` | Reinicializuje s novГғВҪm instrumentem. | `void` |
| `setNoteState(bool isOn, uint8_t velocity = 0)` | `isOn` (true/false), `velocity` (0-127) | `voice.setNoteState(true, 100);` | NastavГғВӯ stav: true = startNote, false = stopNote. | `void` |
| `advancePosition()` | - | `voice.advancePosition();` | Posune pozici o 1 frame (pro non-real-time). | `void` |
| `getCurrentAudioData() const` | - | `AudioData data = voice.getCurrentAudioData();` | VrГғВЎtГғВӯ stereo sample (left/right) s gainem. | `AudioData` |
| `processBlock(AudioBuffer& outputBuffer, int numSamples)` | `outputBuffer`, `numSamples` | `voice.processBlock(buf, 512);` | **HLAVNГғВҚ METODA**: Zpracuje blok, aplikuje obГғВЎlku, zapisuje do bufferu. VrГғВЎtГғВӯ true, pokud aktivnГғВӯ. | `bool` |
| `getMidiNote() const` | - | `uint8_t note = voice.getMidiNote();` | Getter pro MIDI notu. | `uint8_t` |
| `isActive() const` | - | `if (voice.isActive()) { ... }` | Kontroluje aktivitu (gate on nebo releasing). | `bool` |

#### **PГ…в„ўГғВӯklad pouГ…ВҫitГғВӯ VoiceManager:**
```cpp
Logger logger("./");
InstrumentLoader loader(sampler, 44100, logger);
loader.loadInstrument();

// NOVГғвҖ°: Inicializace VoiceManager (pool 128 voice)
VoiceManager manager(128, logger);
manager.initializeAll(loader);  // Inicializuje voices s instrumenty

// NastavenГғВӯ noty (note-on pro MIDI 60, velocity 100)
manager.setNoteState(60, true, 100);

// ProcesovГғВЎnГғВӯ audio bloku (simulace JUCE processBlock)
AudioBuffer output(512);  // Stereo buffer pro 512 samples
if (manager.processBlock(output, 512)) {
    // VГғВҪstup v output.leftChannel a output.rightChannel
    // NapГ…в„ў. pro JUCE: PГ…в„ўidej do reГғВЎlnГғВ©ho AudioBuffer
}

// Note-off
manager.setNoteState(60, false);
```

### Funkce runSampler
- **Signatura**: `int runSampler(Logger& logger)`
- **PГ…в„ўГғВӯklad**: `runSampler(logger);`
- **KomentГғВЎГ…в„ў**: **AKTUALIZOVГғВҒNO**: SpustГғВӯ kompletnГғВӯ workflow vГ„ВҚetnГ„вҖә novГғВ©ho InstrumentLoader. Deleguje prohledГғВЎvГғВЎnГғВӯ do SamplerIO, **inicializuje InstrumentLoader, naГ„ВҚte vГ…ВЎechny samples do pamГ„вҖәti jako stereo buffery**, **NOVГғвҖ°: Inicializuje VoiceManager, nastavГғВӯ test notu (MIDI 108/vel 7), procesuje blok s obГғВЎlkou a loguje stavy**. **Testuje novГғВ© API metody get_sample_begin_pointer(), get_frame_count() atd. i processBlock pro Voice**. Loguje vГ…ВЎechny kroky vГ„ВҚetnГ„вҖә detailnГғВӯch informacГғВӯ o stereo konverzi a JUCE-ready formГғВЎtu. VrГғВЎtГғВӯ 0 pГ…в„ўi ГғВәspГ„вҖәchu (chyby konГ„ВҚГғВӯ `std::exit(1)`). PouГ…Вҫijte pro standalone test s plnou funkcionalitou.

## Struktura projektu
### KlГғВӯГ„ВҚovГғВ© soubory
- **CMakeLists.txt**: Definuje projekt, pГ…в„ўidГғВЎvГғВЎ libsndfile, linkuje soubory (`main.cpp`, `sampler/*.cpp`) a include cesty. **AKTUALIZOVГғВҒNO**: PГ…в„ўidГғВЎny `instrument_loader.h/cpp`, `voice.h/cpp`, `voice_manager.h/cpp`.
- **main.cpp**: HlavnГғВӯ vstup ГўвӮ¬вҖң inicializuje logger, zpracuje argumenty a volГғВЎ `runSampler`.
- **sampler/core_logger.h/cpp**: Implementace tГ…в„ўГғВӯdy `Logger`.
- **sampler/sampler.h/cpp**: Deklarace a implementace funkce `runSampler` a tГ…в„ўГғВӯdy `SamplerIO`.
- **sampler/sampler_io.cpp**: Implementace SamplerIO metod.
- **sampler/instrument_loader.h/cpp**: **NOVГғвҖ°**: Implementace tГ…в„ўГғВӯdy `InstrumentLoader` pro naГ„ВҚГғВӯtГғВЎnГғВӯ do pamГ„вҖәti.
- **sampler/voice.h/cpp**: **NOVГғвҖ°**: Implementace tГ…в„ўГғВӯdy `Voice` pro hlasovou jednotku s obГғВЎlkou a stavy.
- **sampler/voice_manager.h/cpp**: **NOVГғвҖ°**: Implementace tГ…в„ўГғВӯdy `VoiceManager` pro polyfonnГғВӯ management.
- **sampler/wav_file_exporter.h/cpp**: Export WAV pro testovГғВЎnГғВӯ.
- **.vscode/**: Konfigurace pro VS Code (build tasky, launch, settings pro terminal a file associations).
- **README.md**: Tento soubor.

### **NOVГғвҖ°: Struktury a tГ…в„ўГғВӯdy**
#### Struktura `SampleInfo` (v `sampler.h`) - NEZMГ„ЕЎNГ„ЕЎNO
UchovГғВЎvГғВЎ metadata o WAV samplu - bez zmГ„вҖәn, podle freeze requirement.

#### **NOVГғВҒ struktura `Instrument` (v `instrument_loader.h`)** - BEZ ZMГ„ЕЎN
Reprezentuje jeden MIDI note s velocity vrstvami a **novГғВҪmi stereo metadaty** (viz vГғВҪГ…ВЎe).

#### **NOVГғВҒ tГ…в„ўГғВӯda `InstrumentLoader` (v `instrument_loader.h/cpp`)** - BEZ ZMГ„ЕЎN
Centralizuje naГ„ВҚГғВӯtГғВЎnГғВӯ WAV samples do pamГ„вҖәti s klГғВӯГ„ВҚovГғВҪmi vlastnostmi (viz vГғВҪГ…ВЎe).

#### **NOVГғвҖ° tГ…в„ўГғВӯdy `Voice` a `VoiceManager` (v `voice.h/cpp` a `voice_manager.h/cpp`)**
- `Voice`: Spravuje jednu notu s obГғВЎlkou, stavy a pГ…в„ўГғВӯstupem k stereo bufferГ…ВҜm. Podporuje metody pro inicializaci, setNoteState a processBlock.
- `VoiceManager`: Pool voice pro polyfonii, inicializuje voices, nastavuje stavy a procesuje bloky.
- **Simulace JUCE**: `AudioBuffer` pro vГғВҪstup, `AudioData` pro sample data.

#### TГ…в„ўГғВӯda `Logger` (v `core_logger.h/cpp`) - NEZMГ„ЕЎNГ„ЕЎNO
ZГ…ВҜstГғВЎvГғВЎ stejnГғВЎ jako pГ…в„ўed aktualizacГғВӯ.

## Г…ЛңeГ…ВЎenГғВӯ problГғВ©mГ…ВҜ
- **Execution Policy**: SpusГ…ВҘte `Set-ExecutionPolicy RemoteSigned -Scope CurrentUser` v PowerShell.
- **libsndfile chybГғВӯ**: StГғВЎhnГ„вҖәte z [libsndfile GitHub](https://github.com/libsndfile/libsndfile) a upravte CMakeLists.txt.
- **LinkovacГғВӯ chyba LNK1104**: UkonГ„ВҚete vГ…ВЎechny procesy IthacaCore.exe, smaГ…Вҫte build sloГ…Вҫku a sestavte znovu.
- **Logy**: Sledujte `core_logger/core_logger.log`. Pro real-time: `Get-Content -Path "core_logger/core_logger.log" -Tail 10 -Wait`.
- **RozГ…ВЎГғВӯГ…в„ўenГғВӯ**: Upravte cestu v `sampler.cpp` pro jinГғВ© samples. **NOVГғвҖ°: Pro prГғВЎci s naГ„ВҚtenГғВҪmi buffery pouГ…Вҫijte InstrumentLoader API; pro pГ…в„ўehrГғВЎvГғВЎnГғВӯ VoiceManager**.
- **Chyba - nekonzistence frekvence**: Program se ukonГ„ВҚГғВӯ s chybou, pokud frekvence v nГғВЎzvu souboru neodpovГғВӯdГғВЎ frekvenci v WAV headeru.
- **NepodporovanГғВҪ subformГғВЎt**: Program konГ„ВҚГғВӯ s chybou pГ…в„ўi detekci nepodporovanГғВ©ho audio formГғВЎtu.
- **NOVГғвҖ° - Validace stereo**: Program konГ„ВҚГғВӯ s chybou pГ…в„ўi selhГғВЎnГғВӯ validace stereo konzistence v InstrumentLoader.
- **NOVГғвҖ° - Chyba v Voice**: Pokud instrument nenГғВӯ inicializovГғВЎn, processBlock vrГғВЎtГғВӯ false (log warning).

## PoznГғВЎmky
- **NГғВЎzvoslovГғВӯ souborГ…ВҜ**: Samples musГғВӯ mГғВӯt formГғВЎt `mXXX-velY-fZZ.wav` (XXX = MIDI nota 0-127, Y = velocity 0-7, ZZ = zkrГғВЎcenГғВЎ frekvence s 'f' prefixem: f8, f11, f16, f22, f44, f48, f88, f96, f176, f192). Jinak se ignorujГғВӯ s warningem.
- **Validace**: Frekvence v nГғВЎzvu (fZZ) musГғВӯ odpovГғВӯdat frekvenci v WAV headeru, jinak program konГ„ВҚГғВӯ s chybou.
- **NOVГғвҖ° - Stereo formГғВЎt**: **VГ…ВЎechny buffery jsou vГ…Вҫdy uloГ…Вҫeny jako stereo interleaved [L,R,L,R...] bez ohledu na pГ…ВҜvodnГғВӯ formГғВЎt**.
- **NOVГғвҖ° - Mono konverze**: **Mono samples se automaticky duplikujГғВӯ do stereo formГғВЎtu (L=R)** pro jednotnost.
- **NOVГғвҖ° - JUCE optimalizace**: **Buffer layout je optimalizovanГғВҪ pro JUCE AudioBuffer de-interleaving**.
- **Detekce formГғВЎtu**: Program analyzuje, zda je WAV interleaved (standard) a jakГғВҪ mГғВЎ subformГғВЎt (16-bit PCM, float, atd.).
- **PodporovanГғВ© formГғВЎty**: 16-bit PCM, 24-bit PCM, 32-bit PCM, 32-bit float, 64-bit double.
- **OptimГғВЎlnГғВӯ formГғВЎt**: 32-bit float (Г…ВҫГғВЎdnГғВЎ konverze potГ…в„ўebnГғВЎ).
- **NOVГғвҖ° - PamГ„вҖәГ…ВҘovГғВ© nГғВЎroky**: **PamГ„вҖәГ…ВҘovГғВ© nГғВЎroky jsou vyГ…ВЎГ…ВЎГғВӯ - vГ…ВЎechny samples jsou uloГ…Вҫeny jako stereo float buffery**.
- **Chyby**: SelhГғВЎnГғВӯ inicializace (adresГғВЎГ…в„ў, pГ…в„ўГғВӯstup, neplatnГғВҪ index v gettech, nekonzistentnГғВӯ frekvence, nepodporovanГғВҪ formГғВЎt, **validace stereo**, **neinicializovanГғВҪ instrument v Voice**) vede k logu a `std::exit(1)`.
- **Thread-safety**: Pouze logovГғВЎnГғВӯ je chrГғВЎnГ„вҖәno mutexem; sampler nenГғВӯ navrГ…Вҫen pro multi-threading.
- **NOVГғвҖ° - RozГ…ВЎГғВӯГ…в„ўenГғВЎ metadata**: Program nynГғВӯ prohledГғВЎvГғВЎ a poskytuje pГ…в„ўГғВӯstup k dГғВ©lce, poГ„ВҚtu kanГғВЎlГ…ВҜ, stereo detekci, poГ„ВҚtu vzorkГ…ВҜ, formГғВЎtu, potГ…в„ўebГ„вҖә konverze a **novГғВҪm stereo metadatГ…ВҜm**.
- **NOVГғвҖ° - Validace integrity**: **AutomatickГғВЎ validace konzistence vГ…ВЎech naГ„ВҚtenГғВҪch stereo bufferГ…ВҜ**.
- **NOVГғвҖ° - Voice stavy**: PouГ…Вҫijte `isActive()` pro kontrolu, `processBlock` pro renderovГғВЎnГғВӯ.
- **Projekt je pГ…в„ўenositelnГғВҪ**: Pro sloГ…ВҫitГ„вҖәjГ…ВЎГғВӯ aplikace pГ…в„ўidejte JUCE nebo dalГ…ВЎГғВӯ knihovny.

## **NOVГғвҖ°: JUCE Integrace**
InstrumentLoader poskytuje perfektnГғВӯ integraci s JUCE AudioBuffer. **NOVГғвҖ°: Voice procesuje do simulovanГғВ©ho AudioBuffer, kterГғВҪ lze snadno pГ…в„ўevГғВ©st do reГғВЎlnГғВ©ho JUCE bufferu.**

```cpp
// ZГғВӯskГғВЎnГғВӯ stereo dat z InstrumentLoader
Instrument& inst = loader.getInstrumentNote(midiNote);
if (inst.velocityExists[velocity]) {
    float* stereoData = inst.get_sample_begin_pointer(velocity);  // [L,R,L,R...]
    sf_count_t frameCount = inst.get_frame_count(velocity);
    
    // De-interleaving pro JUCE AudioBuffer
    AudioBuffer<float> juceBuffer(2, frameCount);
    float* leftChannel = juceBuffer.getWritePointer(0);
    float* rightChannel = juceBuffer.getWritePointer(1);
    
    for (int frame = 0; frame < frameCount; frame++) {
        leftChannel[frame] = stereoData[frame * 2];         // L kanГғВЎl
        rightChannel[frame] = stereoData[frame * 2 + 1];    // R kanГғВЎl
    }
}

// NOVГғвҖ°: PouГ…ВҫitГғВӯ s Voice pro obГғВЎlku
Voice voice(midiNote, inst, logger);
voice.startNote(velocity);
AudioBuffer simBuf(512);  // Simulace pro test
voice.processBlock(simBuf, 512);  // AplikovГғВЎn gain, vГғВҪstup v simBuf
// PГ…в„ўeveГ„ВҸ simBuf do JUCE bufferu
```
---

```
+---------------------------------------------------+
|                VOICEMANAGER                       |
|  - FixnГғВӯ pool 128 Voice (index = midiNote 0-127)  |
|  - Konstruktor: sampleRate (Hz), Logger           |
|                                                   |
|  initializeAll(InstrumentLoader& loader):         |
|    ProchГғВЎzГғВӯ 128x:                                 |
|      voices_[i].initialize(                      |
|        loader.getInstrumentNote(i),               |
|        sampleRate, logger)                       |
|                                                   |
|  setNoteState(midiNote, isOn, velocity):          |
|    voices_[midiNote].setNoteState(isOn, velocity) |
|                                                   |
|  processBlock(outputBuffer, numSamples):          |
|    Loop 128x:                                     |
|      if (voices_[i].processBlock(...)) {          |
|        Mixdown: SouГ„ВҚet stereo vГғВҪstupГ…ВҜ (L/R)       |
|                  s obГғВЎlkou (gain z Voice)         |
|      }                                            |
+---------------------------------------------------+
                                  |
                                  | (propaguje: sampleRate, Instrument ref)
                                  v
+---------------------------------------------------+
|                    VOICE                           |
|  - Г„Е’leny: midiNote, Instrument*, sampleRate,      |
|            state (Idle/Sustaining/Releasing),     |
|            position (frames), gain (0-1),         |
|            releaseSamples (0.2 * sampleRate)      |
|                                                   |
|  initialize(Instrument& inst, int sampleRate,     |
|              Logger& logger):                     |
|    UloГ…ВҫГғВӯ sampleRate (validace >0),                |
|    inst pointer, vypoГ„ВҚГғВӯtГғВЎ releaseSamples,         |
|    reset na Idle stav                             |
|                                                   |
|  setNoteState(bool isOn, uint8_t velocity):       |
|    Mapuje velocity / 16 na layer (0-7),           |
|    if isOn: state=Sustaining, position=0, gain=1.0|
|    else: state=Releasing, releaseStartPosition=pos|
|                                                   |
|  processBlock(outputBuffer, numSamples):          |
|    Loop numSamples:                               |
|      advancePosition()  // Posun + release gain   |
|      getCurrentAudioData(sample)  // Z bufferu    |
|      PГ…в„ўidГғВЎ do outputBuffer (L/R * gain)           |
|    return isActive()  // !Idle                     |
|                                                   |
|  advancePosition():                               |
|    ++position (do frame_count),                   |
|    if Releasing: gain = 1.0 - (elapsed / release) |
|                                                   |
|  getCurrentAudioData(AudioData& data):            |
|    Z interleaved buffer: data.L = buffer[pos*2]   |
|                         data.R = buffer[pos*2+1]  |
|    applyEnvelope(data.L/R * gain)                 |
+---------------------------------------------------+
                                  |
                                  | (pouГ…ВҫГғВӯvГғВЎ: buffer pointer, frame_count)
                                  v
+---------------------------------------------------+
|                INSTRUMENT (struktura)             |
|  - Pro velocity 0-7:                              |
|    sample_ptr_sampleInfo[vel] (pointer na SampleInfo)|
|    sample_ptr_velocity[vel] (float* stereo buffer)|
|    frame_count_stereo[vel] (poГ„ВҚet L/R pГғВЎrГ…ВҜ)       |
|    total_samples_stereo[vel] (frames * 2)         |
|    was_originally_mono[vel] (true=mono duplikovГғВЎn)|
|                                                   |
|  get_sample_begin_pointer(uint8_t vel):           |
|    if velocityExists[vel]: return buffer pointer  |
|    else: nullptr                                  |
|                                                   |
|  get_frame_count(uint8_t vel):                    |
|    return frame_count_stereo[vel] (stereo frames) |
|                                                   |
|  velocityExists[vel]: Flag existence sample       |
+---------------------------------------------------+
                                  |
                                  | (odkazuje na: metadata)
                                  v
+---------------------------------------------------+
|                SAMPLEINFO (z SamplerIO)           |
|  - Metadata z WAV souboru (libsndfile):           |
|    filename (cesta k .wav)                        |
|    sampleRate (Hz, validovГғВЎno s nГғВЎzvem souboru)   |
|    channels (1=mono | 2=stereo)                   |
|    sample_count (frames, dГғВ©lka / sampleRate)      |
|    needsConversion (PCM ГўвҖ вҖҷ float?)                 |
|    isInterleaved (formГғВЎt dat)                     |
|                                                   |
|  findSampleInSampleList(midi, vel, rate):         |
|    VyhledГғВЎ index v seznamu podle klГғВӯГ„ВҚГ…ВҜ            |
|                                                   |
|  getFilename(index), getChannelCount(index),      |
|  getSampleCount(index):                           |
|    VrГғВЎtГғВӯ metadata pro naГ„ВҚtenГғВӯ v Loaderu           |
|                                                   |
|  Г…ВҪГғВЎdnГғВ© buffery ГўвӮ¬вҖң jen info pro I/O a validaci      |
+---------------------------------------------------+
```

# VysvГ„вҖәtlenГғВӯ frames, samples a bytes v audio kontextu

V audio zpracovГғВЎnГғВӯ (napГ…в„ў. v JUCE nebo libsndfile) se tyto termГғВӯny pouГ…ВҫГғВӯvajГғВӯ pro popis velikosti a struktury audio dat. VysvГ„вҖәtlenГғВӯ v kontextu stereo interleaved formГғВЎt [L,R,L,R...]:

- **Frames**: Г„Е’asovГғВЎ jednotka audio signГғВЎlu, kterГғВЎ obsahuje data pro **vГ…ВЎechny kanГғВЎly v jednom okamГ…Вҫiku**. Pro mono = 1 frame = 1 sample. Pro stereo (2 kanГғВЎly) = 1 frame = 2 samples (levГғВҪ + pravГғВҪ). V logu: **529200 frames** znamenГғВЎ dГғВ©lku zvuku v Г„ВҚasovГғВҪch bodech (napГ…в„ў. pГ…в„ўi 44.1 kHz sample rate = ~12 sekund).

- **Samples**: NejmenГ…ВЎГғВӯ jednotka daty ГўвӮ¬вҖң jedna hodnota pro jeden kanГғВЎl v jednom Г„ВҚasovГғВ©m bodГ„вҖә. V multi-kanГғВЎlovГғВ©m audio (stereo) se "total samples" sГ„ВҚГғВӯtГғВЎ pГ…в„ўes vГ…ВЎechny kanГғВЎly. V logu: **1058400 total samples** = 2 kanГғВЎly ГғвҖ” 529200 frames (kaГ…ВҫdГғВҪ frame mГғВЎ 2 samples).

- **Bytes**: CelkovГғВЎ velikost dat v pamГ„вҖәti (v bytech). ZГғВЎvisГғВӯ na bitovГғВ© hloubce (napГ…в„ў. float = 4 bytes na sample). V logu: **4233600 bytes** = 1058400 samples ГғвҖ” 4 bytes (pravdГ„вҖәpodobnГ„вҖә 32-bit float). To je pro interleaved formГғВЎt, kde data jsou propletenГғВЎ (L,R,L,R...), takГ…Вҫe buffer zabere tolik mГғВӯsta.

# Helper commands

## Grab-Files
```
PowerShell.exe -ExecutionPolicy Bypass -File .\Grab-Files.ps1
```

## Watch log
```
Get-Content -Path "./core_logger/core_logger.log" -Tail 10 -Wait
```

## Git submodule init
```
git submodule update --init --recursive
```

## Pridani submodulu rucne
```
git submodule add https://github.com/libsndfile/libsndfile libsndfile
```

## Grep z logu

```
# Sleduje log soubor v reГғВЎlnГғВ©m Г„ВҚase a filtruje Г…в„ўГғВЎdky obsahujГғВӯcГғВӯ "VoiceManagerTester"
Get-Content -Path "C:\Users\jindr\IthacaCore\build\Debug\Debug\core_logger\core_logger.log" -Tail 10 -Wait | 
Where-Object { $_ -match "VoiceManagerTester" }
```
